- [ ] **Step 3: Implement MainWindowViewModel.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModel.cs`:

```csharp
using CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.ComponentModel;
using GitDelta.Core.Cli;
using GitDelta.Core.Git;
using GitDelta.Core.Settings;

namespace GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;

/// <summary>
/// Top-level content host. Routes the launch action to either the start
/// screen (<see cref="StartViewModel"/>) or the workspace
/// (<see cref="ShellViewModel"/>), and swaps content when the user opens a
/// different repository.
/// </summary>
public partial class MainWindowViewModel : ObservableObject
{
    private readonly IGitReader _gitReader;
    private readonly ISettingsStore _settings;
    private readonly Func<StartViewModel> _startFactory;
    private readonly Func<ShellViewModel> _shellFactory;

    public MainWindowViewModel(
        IGitReader gitReader,
        ISettingsStore settings,
        Func<StartViewModel> startFactory,
        Func<ShellViewModel> shellFactory)
    {
        _gitReader = gitReader;
        _settings = settings;
        _startFactory = startFactory;
        _shellFactory = shellFactory;
    }

    [ObservableProperty]
    private ObservableObject? _currentContent;

    /// <summary>
    /// Routes the parsed launch action. PrintHelp/PrintVersion are handled by
    /// the bootstrap before the window appears, so here they fall through to
    /// the start screen. OpenRepoWorkingTree resolves the repo root; if it is
    /// not a repository, falls back to the start screen.
    /// </summary>
    public async Task InitializeAsync(LaunchAction action, CancellationToken ct)
    {
        switch (action.Kind)
        {
            case LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree:
                string start = action.RepoPath ?? Directory.GetCurrentDirectory();
                string? root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(start, ct);
                if (root is null)
                {
                    await ShowStartAsync();
                }
                else
                {
                    await OpenRepositoryAsync(root);
                }
                break;

            case LaunchActionKind.ShowStartScreen:
            case LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp:
            case LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion:
            default:
                await ShowStartAsync();
                break;
        }
    }

    /// <summary>Shows the start screen and wires its repository-selected event.</summary>
    public Task ShowStartAsync()
    {
        StartViewModel start = _startFactory();
        start.RepositorySelected += OnRepositorySelected;
        CurrentContent = start;
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    /// <summary>Loads the repository at <paramref name="repoRoot"/> into the shell.</summary>
    public async Task OpenRepositoryAsync(string repoRoot)
    {
        ShellViewModel shell = _shellFactory();
        shell.RepositoryOpenRequested += OnShellRepositoryOpenRequested;
        CurrentContent = shell;
        await shell.LoadRepositoryAsync(repoRoot, CancellationToken.None);
    }

    private async void OnRepositorySelected(string folder)
    {
        string? root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(folder, CancellationToken.None);
        await OpenRepositoryAsync(root ?? folder);
    }

    private async void OnShellRepositoryOpenRequested(string folder)
    {
        string? root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(folder, CancellationToken.None);
        await OpenRepositoryAsync(root ?? folder);
    }
}
```

> Note the `using System.IO;` is supplied by `ImplicitUsings` for `Directory`; if `TreatWarningsAsErrors` flags it as ambiguous it is already covered. If the build complains `Directory` is not found, add `using System.IO;` at the top.

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**

```powershell
dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~MainWindowViewModelTests"
```

Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 7`. If `StartScreen_RepositorySelected_OpensThatRepository` is flaky because of the `async void` event handler, the `await Task.Yield()` in the test plus the synchronous (mocked, completed) `FindRepositoryRootAsync` make the continuation run before the assertion; if it still races, the mock returning a completed `Task` from `Returns(...)` guarantees synchronous completion.

```powershell
git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'
feat(ui): add MainWindowViewModel routing start screen vs shell

InitializeAsync routes each LaunchActionKind; OpenRepoWorkingTree resolves
the repo root and falls back to the start screen when the path is not a repo.
OpenRepositoryAsync loads the shell; start-screen and shell open events both
re-resolve and switch repositories.

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
```

## Phase 7: UI — AvalonEdit Diff Control & Renderers

This phase builds the read-only diff rendering surface. AvalonEdit text rendering, background painting, margin drawing, and scroll-sync are **not unit-testable** (they require a live WPF visual tree and a windowed render pass), so every task here uses **implementation + `dotnet build` + a manual run-and-observe verification**, never a fake unit test. The Core diff model (`FileDiff`, `DiffHunk`, `DiffLine`, `IntraSpan`) from earlier phases is the single source of truth fed into this control.

Task 7.1 ships an **MVP escape hatch** (DiffPlex.Wpf) so the shell is wireable immediately; Tasks 7.2–7.9 build the real AvalonEdit `DiffView` per the BACKBONE contract; Phase 8 layers TextMate syntax on top.

### Task 7.1: MVP fallback — DiffPlex.Wpf SideBySideDiffViewer host control

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml.cs`
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`

This is the documented MVP escape hatch from spec §8: ship DiffPlex.Wpf's `SideBySideDiffViewer` first so the shell has a working diff pane before the bespoke AvalonEdit `DiffView` (Task 7.2+) is finished. The Core `FileDiff` model is reused: we reconstruct old/new text from the hunks and let DiffPlex.Wpf re-diff for display. When the real `DiffView` is ready, the shell swaps the control and deletes this file; nothing in Core changes.

- [ ] **Step 1: Pin the DiffPlex.Wpf package version centrally**

  Add the WPF rendering package alongside the existing DiffPlex core entry in central package management. Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props` and add the `PackageVersion` line inside the existing `<ItemGroup>`:

  ```xml
  <PackageVersion Include="DiffPlex.Wpf" Version="1.4.4" />
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Reference DiffPlex.Wpf from the UI project**

  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` and add inside the package `<ItemGroup>` (version omitted — central management supplies it):

  ```xml
  <PackageReference Include="DiffPlex.Wpf" />
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3: Add a static text reconstructor that turns a FileDiff into old/new text**

  DiffPlex.Wpf wants two plain strings. We rebuild them from the hunks: deleted+context lines form the "old" side, added+context lines form the "new" side. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml.cs` with this complete content (XAML follows in Step 4):

  ```csharp
  using System.Text;
  using System.Windows;
  using System.Windows.Controls;
  using GitDelta.Core.Models;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls;

  /// <summary>
  /// MVP escape hatch (spec §8): hosts DiffPlex.Wpf's SideBySideDiffViewer.
  /// Reconstructs old/new text from the Core FileDiff hunks and lets DiffPlex.Wpf
  /// re-diff for display. Replaced by the AvalonEdit DiffView (Task 7.2+).
  /// </summary>
  public partial class MvpDiffView : UserControl
  {
      public static readonly DependencyProperty FileDiffProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(FileDiff), typeof(FileDiff), typeof(MvpDiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(null, OnFileDiffChanged));

      public FileDiff? FileDiff
      {
          get => (FileDiff?)GetValue(FileDiffProperty);
          set => SetValue(FileDiffProperty, value);
      }

      public MvpDiffView()
      {
          InitializeComponent();
      }

      private static void OnFileDiffChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)
      {
          ((MvpDiffView)d).Render((FileDiff?)e.NewValue);
      }

      private void Render(FileDiff? diff)
      {
          if (diff is null)
          {
              Viewer.OldText = string.Empty;
              Viewer.NewText = string.Empty;
              return;
          }

          if (diff.IsBinary)
          {
              Viewer.OldText = "(binary file — no textual diff)";
              Viewer.NewText = "(binary file — no textual diff)";
              return;
          }

          var (oldText, newText) = Reconstruct(diff);
          Viewer.OldText = oldText;
          Viewer.NewText = newText;

          if (diff.IsTruncated)
          {
              Viewer.NewText += Environment.NewLine + "… (diff truncated — file too large)";
          }
      }

      private static (string OldText, string NewText) Reconstruct(FileDiff diff)
      {
          var oldSb = new StringBuilder();
          var newSb = new StringBuilder();
          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)
          {
              foreach (DiffLine line in hunk.Lines)
              {
                  switch (line.Kind)
                  {
                      case DiffLineKind.Context:
                          oldSb.AppendLine(line.Text);
                          newSb.AppendLine(line.Text);
                          break;
                      case DiffLineKind.Deleted:
                          oldSb.AppendLine(line.Text);
                          break;
                      case DiffLineKind.Added:
                          newSb.AppendLine(line.Text);
                          break;
                  }
              }
          }

          return (oldSb.ToString(), newSb.ToString());
      }
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4: Add the XAML that hosts the DiffPlex.Wpf viewer**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml`:

  ```xml
  <UserControl
      x:Class="GitDelta.UI.Controls.MvpDiffView"
      xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"
      xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml"
      xmlns:diffwpf="clr-namespace:DiffPlex.Wpf.Controls;assembly=DiffPlex.Wpf">
      <Grid Background="{DynamicResource ApplicationBackgroundBrush}">
          <diffwpf:SideBySideDiffViewer x:Name="Viewer" />
      </Grid>
  </UserControl>
  ```

- [ ] **Step 5: Build the UI project**

  Run from `C:/code/projects/GitDelta`:

  ```powershell
  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj
  ```

  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. (Note: `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true` means any nullable or obsolete warning fails the build — there should be none here.)

  ```powershell

  git commit -m @'

  Hosts SideBySideDiffViewer, reconstructing old/new text from the Core
  FileDiff model. Lets the shell wire a working diff pane before the
  bespoke AvalonEdit DiffView lands. Binary and truncated fallbacks included.

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Reference AvalonEdit and allow net6.0-windows forward-compat**

With `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true` (spec §15 risk) we scope a `NoWarn` to keep zero-warning builds. In `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` add inside the package `<ItemGroup>`:

  ```xml

  ```

  Then add a dedicated property group at the end of the same csproj (before `</Project>`):

  ```xml
  <PropertyGroup>
    <!-- AvalonEdit 6.x ships net6.0-windows assemblies; loads forward-compat on net10.
         Scope-suppress the cross-targeting restore warning only (spec §15 risk). -->
    <NoWarn>$(NoWarn);NU1701</NoWarn>
  </PropertyGroup>
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3: Create the DiffView code-behind with every dependency property + method stubs**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`. This is the complete contract surface; private fields reference the two named editors from the XAML (Step 4):

  ```csharp
  using System.Windows;
  using System.Windows.Controls;
  using GitDelta.Core.Models;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls;

  /// <summary>
  /// Read-only AvalonEdit-based diff renderer. SideBySide uses two editors with
  /// filler/imaginary lines and mirrored scroll; Unified uses a single editor.
  /// Backbone contract: 7 dependency properties + GoToNextChange / GoToPreviousChange
  /// / ShowFind / CopySelection.
  /// </summary>
  public partial class DiffView : UserControl
  {
      public DiffView()
      {
          InitializeComponent();
      }

      #region FileDiff
      public static readonly DependencyProperty FileDiffProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(FileDiff), typeof(FileDiff), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(null, OnRenderInputChanged));

      public FileDiff? FileDiff
      {
          get => (FileDiff?)GetValue(FileDiffProperty);
          set => SetValue(FileDiffProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      #region ViewMode
      public static readonly DependencyProperty ViewModeProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(ViewMode), typeof(DiffViewMode), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(DiffViewMode.SideBySide, OnRenderInputChanged));

      public DiffViewMode ViewMode
      {
          get => (DiffViewMode)GetValue(ViewModeProperty);
          set => SetValue(ViewModeProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      #region ShowWhitespace
      public static readonly DependencyProperty ShowWhitespaceProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(ShowWhitespace), typeof(bool), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(false, OnDisplayOptionChanged));

      public bool ShowWhitespace
      {
          get => (bool)GetValue(ShowWhitespaceProperty);
          set => SetValue(ShowWhitespaceProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      #region WordWrap
      public static readonly DependencyProperty WordWrapProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(WordWrap), typeof(bool), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(false, OnDisplayOptionChanged));

      public bool WordWrap
      {
          get => (bool)GetValue(WordWrapProperty);
          set => SetValue(WordWrapProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      #region TabSize
      public static readonly DependencyProperty TabSizeProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(TabSize), typeof(int), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(4, OnDisplayOptionChanged));

      public int TabSize
      {
          get => (int)GetValue(TabSizeProperty);
          set => SetValue(TabSizeProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      #region SyntaxLanguageId
      public static readonly DependencyProperty SyntaxLanguageIdProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(SyntaxLanguageId), typeof(string), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(null, OnSyntaxChanged));

      public string? SyntaxLanguageId
      {
          get => (string?)GetValue(SyntaxLanguageIdProperty);
          set => SetValue(SyntaxLanguageIdProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      #region IsDarkTheme
      public static readonly DependencyProperty IsDarkThemeProperty =
          DependencyProperty.Register(
              nameof(IsDarkTheme), typeof(bool), typeof(DiffView),
              new PropertyMetadata(false, OnSyntaxChanged));

      public bool IsDarkTheme
      {
          get => (bool)GetValue(IsDarkThemeProperty);
          set => SetValue(IsDarkThemeProperty, value);
      }
      #endregion

      // --- Public methods (called by the diff toolbar in the shell) ---
      public void GoToNextChange() { }
      public void GoToPreviousChange() { }
      public void ShowFind() { }
      public void CopySelection() { }

      // --- Change callbacks (wired in later tasks) ---
      private static void OnRenderInputChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e) { }
      private static void OnDisplayOptionChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e) { }
      private static void OnSyntaxChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e) { }

      // Editors named in XAML; used by later tasks.
      private TextEditor LeftEditorRef => LeftEditor;
      private TextEditor RightEditorRef => RightEditor;
      private TextEditor UnifiedEditorRef => UnifiedEditor;
  }
  ```

### Task 7.3: Build the display document + per-line classification model from FileDiff

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffRowKind.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentModel.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentBuilder.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/DiffDocumentBuilderTests.cs`

The renderers, change-bar margin, and intra-line colorizer all need a precomputed, indexed lookup of "for display line N, what kind of change is this and what intra-spans apply" (spec §8: "DiffPlex line classification precomputed once into an indexed lookup"). This builder is **pure C# with no WPF dependency**, so it IS unit-testable — follow TDD here. It produces, for each compare mode, the document text plus a per-document-line classification array, including filler lines for side-by-side alignment.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the row-kind enum and document model record**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffRowKind.cs`:

  ```csharp
  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>Per-display-line classification used by renderers/margin/colorizer.</summary>
  public enum DiffRowKind
  {
      Context,
      Added,
      Deleted,
      Modified,
      /// <summary>Imaginary/filler row that exists only to keep the two split sides aligned.</summary>
      Filler,
  }
  ```

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentModel.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using GitDelta.Core.Models;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>One display line in a built diff document.</summary>
  public sealed record DiffRow(
      DiffRowKind Kind,
      string Text,
      int? OldLineNumber,
      int? NewLineNumber,
      IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> IntraSpans);

  /// <summary>
  /// A fully built side of a diff document: the joined text (one <see cref="DiffRow"/>
  /// per line) plus the indexed per-line classification. Document line numbers are 1-based;
  /// Rows[0] corresponds to AvalonEdit line 1.
  /// </summary>
  public sealed record DiffDocumentSide(string Text, IReadOnlyList<DiffRow> Rows);

  /// <summary>
  /// Result of building a document for a compare mode. For Unified, only
  /// <see cref="Unified"/> is populated; for SideBySide, <see cref="Left"/> and
  /// <see cref="Right"/> are populated and are guaranteed equal in row count.
  /// </summary>
  public sealed record DiffDocumentModel(
      DiffDocumentSide? Unified,
      DiffDocumentSide? Left,
      DiffDocumentSide? Right);
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing test for the builder**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/DiffDocumentBuilderTests.cs`. These exercise filler-line alignment (the core correctness concern) and unified inlining:

  ```csharp
  using GitDelta.Core.Models;
  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;
  using Shouldly;
  using Xunit;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.Controls;

  public sealed class DiffDocumentBuilderTests
  {
      private static FileDiff MakeDiff(params DiffLine[] lines)
      {
          var hunk = new DiffHunk(1, 0, 1, 0, "@@ -1 +1 @@", lines);
          var file = new ChangedFile("a.cs", null, ChangeKind.Modified, 1, 1, false);
          return new FileDiff(file, new[] { hunk }, IsBinary: false, IsTruncated: false);
      }

      private static DiffLine Ctx(string t, int oldN, int newN) =>
          new(DiffLineKind.Context, oldN, newN, t, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());

      private static DiffLine Del(string t, int oldN) =>
          new(DiffLineKind.Deleted, oldN, null, t, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());

      private static DiffLine Add(string t, int newN) =>
          new(DiffLineKind.Added, null, newN, t, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());

      [Fact]
      public void SideBySide_aligns_unequal_runs_with_filler_rows()
      {
          // one deletion, two additions => right side gets the extra add,
          // left side gets a filler to stay aligned.
          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(
              Ctx("ctx", 1, 1),
              Del("gone", 2),
              Add("new1", 2),
              Add("new2", 3));

          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide);

          model.Left.ShouldNotBeNull();
          model.Right.ShouldNotBeNull();
          model.Left!.Rows.Count.ShouldBe(model.Right!.Rows.Count);

          // Row 0 = context on both sides.
          model.Left.Rows[0].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Context);
          model.Right.Rows[0].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Context);

          // Row 1: left deleted "gone", right modified "new1".
          model.Left.Rows[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Deleted);
          model.Left.Rows[1].Text.ShouldBe("gone");
          model.Right.Rows[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Modified);
          model.Right.Rows[1].Text.ShouldBe("new1");

          // Row 2: left filler, right added "new2".
          model.Left.Rows[2].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Filler);
          model.Left.Rows[2].Text.ShouldBe(string.Empty);
          model.Right.Rows[2].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Added);
          model.Right.Rows[2].Text.ShouldBe("new2");
      }

      [Fact]
      public void SideBySide_text_has_one_line_per_row()
      {
          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(Ctx("a", 1, 1), Del("b", 2), Add("c", 2));
          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide);

          model.Left!.Text.Split('\n').Length.ShouldBe(model.Left.Rows.Count);
          model.Right!.Text.Split('\n').Length.ShouldBe(model.Right.Rows.Count);
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Unified_inlines_deletes_then_adds_in_order()
      {
          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(Ctx("a", 1, 1), Del("b", 2), Add("c", 2));
          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.Unified);

          model.Unified.ShouldNotBeNull();
          model.Left.ShouldBeNull();
          model.Right.ShouldBeNull();

          model.Unified!.Rows.Select(r => r.Kind).ShouldBe(new[]
          {
              DiffRowKind.Context, DiffRowKind.Deleted, DiffRowKind.Added,
          });
          model.Unified.Rows[1].Text.ShouldBe("b");
          model.Unified.Rows[2].Text.ShouldBe("c");
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Modified_pair_keeps_intra_spans_on_both_sides()
      {
          var delSpans = new[] { new IntraSpan(0, 4, IntraSpanKind.Deleted) };
          var addSpans = new[] { new IntraSpan(0, 3, IntraSpanKind.Added) };
          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(
              new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Deleted, 1, null, "gone", delSpans),
              new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Added, null, 1, "new", addSpans));

          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide);

          model.Left!.Rows[0].IntraSpans.ShouldBe(delSpans);
          model.Right!.Rows[0].IntraSpans.ShouldBe(addSpans);
      }
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2 (run): Run the test and watch it fail to compile**

  ```powershell
  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffDocumentBuilderTests"
  ```

  Expected: **build error** — `DiffDocumentBuilder` does not exist yet (`CS0103`/`The name 'DiffDocumentBuilder' does not exist`). This is the expected red state.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement the builder**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentBuilder.cs`. The alignment rule mirrors spec §8: within a hunk, consecutive deleted lines pair 1:1 with the following added lines (those pairs render as `Modified`); leftover deletes/adds get filler on the opposite side.

  ```csharp
  using System.Text;
  using GitDelta.Core.Models;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>
  /// Builds the display document(s) and per-line classification once from a FileDiff
  /// (spec §8 indexed lookup). Pure C#, no WPF — unit-tested.
  /// </summary>
  public static class DiffDocumentBuilder
  {
      private static readonly IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> NoSpans = Array.Empty<IntraSpan>();

      public static DiffDocumentModel Build(FileDiff diff, DiffViewMode mode) =>
          mode == DiffViewMode.Unified ? BuildUnified(diff) : BuildSideBySide(diff);

      private static DiffDocumentModel BuildUnified(FileDiff diff)
      {
          var rows = new List<DiffRow>();
          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)
          {
              foreach (DiffLine line in hunk.Lines)
              {
                  DiffRowKind kind = line.Kind switch
                  {
                      DiffLineKind.Added => DiffRowKind.Added,
                      DiffLineKind.Deleted => DiffRowKind.Deleted,
                      _ => DiffRowKind.Context,
                  };
                  rows.Add(new DiffRow(kind, line.Text, line.OldLineNumber, line.NewLineNumber, line.IntraSpans));
              }
          }

          return new DiffDocumentModel(ToSide(rows), Left: null, Right: null);
      }

      private static DiffDocumentModel BuildSideBySide(FileDiff diff)
      {
          var left = new List<DiffRow>();
          var right = new List<DiffRow>();

          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)
          {
              // Group consecutive deleted/added runs so we can pair them 1:1.
              int i = 0;
              IReadOnlyList<DiffLine> lines = hunk.Lines;
              while (i < lines.Count)
              {
                  DiffLine line = lines[i];
                  if (line.Kind == DiffLineKind.Context)
                  {
                      left.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Context, line.Text, line.OldLineNumber, line.NewLineNumber, line.IntraSpans));
                      right.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Context, line.Text, line.OldLineNumber, line.NewLineNumber, line.IntraSpans));
                      i++;
                      continue;
                  }

                  int delStart = i;
                  while (i < lines.Count && lines[i].Kind == DiffLineKind.Deleted)
                  {
                      i++;
                  }

                  int addStart = i;
                  while (i < lines.Count && lines[i].Kind == DiffLineKind.Added)
                  {
                      i++;
                  }

                  EmitRun(lines, delStart, addStart, i, left, right);
              }
          }

          PadToEqual(left, right);
          return new DiffDocumentModel(Unified: null, ToSide(left), ToSide(right));
      }

      private static void EmitRun(
          IReadOnlyList<DiffLine> lines, int delStart, int addStart, int end,
          List<DiffRow> left, List<DiffRow> right)
      {
          int delCount = addStart - delStart;
          int addCount = end - addStart;
          int pairs = Math.Min(delCount, addCount);

          // Paired lines => Modified on both sides (intra-spans carry through).
          for (int p = 0; p < pairs; p++)
          {
              DiffLine d = lines[delStart + p];
              DiffLine a = lines[addStart + p];
              left.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Modified, d.Text, d.OldLineNumber, null, d.IntraSpans));
              right.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Modified, a.Text, null, a.NewLineNumber, a.IntraSpans));
          }

          // Leftover deletions: left=Deleted, right=Filler.
          for (int p = pairs; p < delCount; p++)
          {
              DiffLine d = lines[delStart + p];
              left.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Deleted, d.Text, d.OldLineNumber, null, NoSpans));
              right.Add(Filler());
          }

          // Leftover additions: left=Filler, right=Added.
          for (int p = pairs; p < addCount; p++)
          {
              DiffLine a = lines[addStart + p];
              left.Add(Filler());
              right.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Added, a.Text, null, a.NewLineNumber, NoSpans));
          }
      }

      private static DiffRow Filler() =>
          new(DiffRowKind.Filler, string.Empty, null, null, NoSpans);

      private static void PadToEqual(List<DiffRow> left, List<DiffRow> right)
      {
          while (left.Count < right.Count)
          {
              left.Add(Filler());
          }

          while (right.Count < left.Count)
          {
              right.Add(Filler());
          }
      }

      private static DiffDocumentSide ToSide(IReadOnlyList<DiffRow> rows)
      {
          var sb = new StringBuilder();
          for (int r = 0; r < rows.Count; r++)
          {
              if (r > 0)
              {
                  sb.Append('\n');
              }

              sb.Append(rows[r].Text);
          }

          return new DiffDocumentSide(sb.ToString(), rows);
      }
  }
  ```

### Task 7.4: Diff brush palette bound to WPF-UI DynamicResource keys

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffBrushes.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml`
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`

The renderers need semi-transparent add/delete/modify backgrounds, solid intra-span tints, and change-bar colors that read correctly over the Mica backdrop and adapt to theme (spec §8: "semi-transparent diff backgrounds so Mica/selection still read"; "editor brushes bound to WPF-UI DynamicResource keys"). We define a resource dictionary of brushes and a tiny C# accessor that resolves them at render time so theme swaps re-color the diff without rebuilding documents.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the brush resource dictionary**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml`. Alpha values keep backgrounds translucent so Mica shows through; intra (word) tints are stronger. The keys are referenced by name from `DiffBrushes.cs`:

  ```xml
  <ResourceDictionary
      xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"
      xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml">

      <!-- Full-line backgrounds (semi-transparent so Mica/selection read through) -->
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffAddedLineBrush"    Color="#3322C55E" />
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffDeletedLineBrush"  Color="#33EF4444" />
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffModifiedLineBrush" Color="#33F59E0B" />
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffFillerLineBrush"   Color="#14808080" />

      <!-- Intra-line (word-level) tints, layered over the line background -->
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffAddedSpanBrush"   Color="#5522C55E" />
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffDeletedSpanBrush" Color="#55EF4444" />

      <!-- Change-bar margin colors (solid) -->
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffAddedBarBrush"    Color="#FF22C55E" />
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffDeletedBarBrush"  Color="#FFEF4444" />
      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffModifiedBarBrush" Color="#FFF59E0B" />
  </ResourceDictionary>
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Merge the dictionary into App resources**

  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml` and add the dictionary to the existing `<ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>` (it already merges the WPF-UI theme/control dictionaries — add ours after them so our keys win):

  ```xml
  <ResourceDictionary Source="pack://application:,,,/GitDelta.UI;component/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml" />
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3: Create a C# accessor that resolves brushes by key at render time**

  Renderers run on the UI thread and need `System.Windows.Media.Brush` instances; resolving from `Application.Current.Resources` each render keeps theme swaps live. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffBrushes.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using System.Windows;
  using System.Windows.Media;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>
  /// Resolves diff render brushes from merged application resources by key.
  /// Resolving live (not caching) lets theme swaps recolor the diff (spec §8).
  /// Falls back to hard-coded brushes if a key is missing (e.g. design-time).
  /// </summary>
  public static class DiffBrushes
  {
      public static Brush AddedLine => Resolve("DiffAddedLineBrush", 0x33, 0x22, 0xC5, 0x5E);
      public static Brush DeletedLine => Resolve("DiffDeletedLineBrush", 0x33, 0xEF, 0x44, 0x44);
      public static Brush ModifiedLine => Resolve("DiffModifiedLineBrush", 0x33, 0xF5, 0x9E, 0x0B);
      public static Brush FillerLine => Resolve("DiffFillerLineBrush", 0x14, 0x80, 0x80, 0x80);

      public static Brush AddedSpan => Resolve("DiffAddedSpanBrush", 0x55, 0x22, 0xC5, 0x5E);
      public static Brush DeletedSpan => Resolve("DiffDeletedSpanBrush", 0x55, 0xEF, 0x44, 0x44);

      public static Brush AddedBar => Resolve("DiffAddedBarBrush", 0xFF, 0x22, 0xC5, 0x5E);
      public static Brush DeletedBar => Resolve("DiffDeletedBarBrush", 0xFF, 0xEF, 0x44, 0x44);
      public static Brush ModifiedBar => Resolve("DiffModifiedBarBrush", 0xFF, 0xF5, 0x9E, 0x0B);

      private static Brush Resolve(string key, byte a, byte r, byte g, byte b)
      {
          if (Application.Current?.TryFindResource(key) is Brush brush)
          {
              return brush;
          }

          var fallback = new SolidColorBrush(Color.FromArgb(a, r, g, b));
          fallback.Freeze();
          return fallback;
      }
  }
  ```


### Task 7.5: Full-line background renderer (IBackgroundRenderer)

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffLineBackgroundRenderer.cs`

Per spec §8 / BACKBONE: a custom `IBackgroundRenderer` paints full-line add/delete/modify (and filler) backgrounds using `BackgroundGeometryBuilder`. It reads its classification from the `DiffDocumentSide.Rows` array (built in 7.3), indexing by AvalonEdit document line number. This is pure rendering — **manual verification only**.

- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the background renderer**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffLineBackgroundRenderer.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using System.Windows;
  using System.Windows.Media;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>
  /// Paints full-line add/delete/modify/filler backgrounds behind the text,
  /// driven by the precomputed per-line classification. Operates only on visible
  /// lines (AvalonEdit virtualization).
  /// </summary>
  public sealed class DiffLineBackgroundRenderer : IBackgroundRenderer
  {
      private DiffDocumentSide? _side;

      public KnownLayer Layer => KnownLayer.Background;

      public void SetSide(DiffDocumentSide? side)
      {
          _side = side;
      }

      public void Draw(TextView textView, DrawingContext drawingContext)
      {
          DiffDocumentSide? side = _side;
          if (side is null || textView.VisualLinesValid == false)
          {
              return;
          }

          textView.EnsureVisualLines();

          foreach (VisualLine vl in textView.VisualLines)
          {
              int docLine = vl.FirstDocumentLine.LineNumber; // 1-based
              int rowIndex = docLine - 1;
              if (rowIndex < 0 || rowIndex >= side.Rows.Count)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              Brush? brush = side.Rows[rowIndex].Kind switch
              {
                  DiffRowKind.Added => DiffBrushes.AddedLine,
                  DiffRowKind.Deleted => DiffBrushes.DeletedLine,
                  DiffRowKind.Modified => DiffBrushes.ModifiedLine,
                  DiffRowKind.Filler => DiffBrushes.FillerLine,
                  _ => null,
              };

              if (brush is null)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              var geoBuilder = new BackgroundGeometryBuilder
              {
                  AlignToWholePixels = true,
                  CornerRadius = 0,
              };

              foreach (Rect rect in BackgroundGeometryBuilder.GetRectsForSegment(
                  textView, vl.FirstDocumentLine, extendToFullWidthAtLineEnd: true))
              {
                  var full = new Rect(0, rect.Top, textView.ActualWidth, rect.Height);
                  geoBuilder.AddRectangle(textView, new RectSegment(full));
              }

              Geometry geometry = geoBuilder.CreateGeometry();
              if (geometry is not null)
              {
                  drawingContext.DrawGeometry(brush, null, geometry);
              }
          }
      }

      /// <summary>Adapts a raw Rect to the ISegment-on-textview API of the geometry builder.</summary>
      private sealed class RectSegment : ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document.ISegment
      {
          private readonly Rect _rect;
          public RectSegment(Rect rect) => _rect = rect;

          // Not used for pixel-rect geometry, but required by the interface.
          public int Offset => 0;
          public int Length => 0;
          public int EndOffset => 0;

          public Rect Rect => _rect;
      }
  }
  ```

  > Implementation note: AvalonEdit's `BackgroundGeometryBuilder.AddRectangle(TextView, ISegment)` resolves segment offsets to rectangles internally; for full-width line fills the simplest robust approach is `AddRectangle(double x, double y, double width, double height)` from the per-line `Rect`. If your AvalonEdit build exposes `geoBuilder.AddRectangle(full.Left, full.Top, full.Width, full.Height)` directly, prefer that overload and delete the `RectSegment` helper. Verify which overload exists in 6.3.1.120 during Step 2.

- [ ] **Step 2: Reconcile the geometry API against AvalonEdit 6.3.1.120 and simplify**

  Open the AvalonEdit assembly metadata to confirm the available overload, then prefer the direct-rect overload. Replace the inner `foreach`/`RectSegment` block in `Draw` with the simpler, definitely-present overload:

  ```csharp
              var geoBuilder = new BackgroundGeometryBuilder { AlignToWholePixels = true };
              foreach (Rect rect in BackgroundGeometryBuilder.GetRectsForSegment(
                  textView, vl.FirstDocumentLine, extendToFullWidthAtLineEnd: true))
              {
                  geoBuilder.AddRectangle(
                      textView,
                      new ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document.TextSegment
                      {
                          StartOffset = vl.FirstDocumentLine.Offset,
                          Length = vl.FirstDocumentLine.Length,
                      });
                  break; // one segment per line is enough; full-width handled below
              }

              Geometry? geometry = geoBuilder.CreateGeometry();
              if (geometry is not null)
              {
                  drawingContext.DrawGeometry(brush, null, geometry);
              }
  ```

  Then delete the `RectSegment` nested class. This uses only public, version-stable APIs (`GetRectsForSegment`, `AddRectangle(TextView, ISegment)`, `TextSegment`). Build to confirm the API resolves:

  ```powershell
  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj
  ```

  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Commit**

  ```powershell

  git commit -m @'
  feat(ui): add full-line diff background renderer

  IBackgroundRenderer that paints add/delete/modify/filler line backgrounds
  via BackgroundGeometryBuilder over visible lines only, driven by the
  precomputed per-line classification.

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
  ```

### Task 7.6: Change-bar margin + intra-line colorizing transformer

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/ChangeBarMargin.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/IntraLineColorizer.cs`

Two more per-line render components: a thin **change-bar margin** drawing the green/red/orange gutter stripe (BACKBONE / spec §8), and a `DocumentColorizingTransformer` that applies the intra-span tints from the model. The colorizer is added to the editor's `LineTransformers` *after* the syntax transformer (Phase 8), so its background tint layers on top of syntax foreground colors. Manual verification only.

- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the change-bar margin**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/ChangeBarMargin.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using System.Windows;
  using System.Windows.Media;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Editing;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>
  /// A narrow gutter margin that draws a solid change-bar (green/red/orange)
  /// for each added/deleted/modified line, driven by the per-line classification.
  /// </summary>
  public sealed class ChangeBarMargin : AbstractMargin
  {
      private const double BarWidth = 4.0;
      private DiffDocumentSide? _side;

      public void SetSide(DiffDocumentSide? side)
      {
          _side = side;
          InvalidateVisual();
      }

      protected override Size MeasureOverride(Size availableSize) => new(BarWidth, 0);

      protected override void OnRender(DrawingContext drawingContext)
      {
          base.OnRender(drawingContext);

          TextView? textView = TextView;
          DiffDocumentSide? side = _side;
          if (textView is null || side is null || textView.VisualLinesValid == false)
          {
              return;
          }

          foreach (VisualLine vl in textView.VisualLines)
          {
              int rowIndex = vl.FirstDocumentLine.LineNumber - 1;
              if (rowIndex < 0 || rowIndex >= side.Rows.Count)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              Brush? brush = side.Rows[rowIndex].Kind switch
              {
                  DiffRowKind.Added => DiffBrushes.AddedBar,
                  DiffRowKind.Deleted => DiffBrushes.DeletedBar,
                  DiffRowKind.Modified => DiffBrushes.ModifiedBar,
                  _ => null,
              };

              if (brush is null)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              double top = vl.VisualTop - textView.VerticalOffset;
              double height = vl.Height;
              drawingContext.DrawRectangle(brush, null, new Rect(0, top, BarWidth, height));
          }
      }

      protected override void OnTextViewChanged(TextView oldTextView, TextView newTextView)
      {
          if (oldTextView is not null)
          {
              oldTextView.VisualLinesChanged -= OnVisualLinesChanged;
          }

          base.OnTextViewChanged(oldTextView, newTextView);

          if (newTextView is not null)
          {
              newTextView.VisualLinesChanged += OnVisualLinesChanged;
          }

          InvalidateVisual();
      }

      private void OnVisualLinesChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e) => InvalidateVisual();
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the intra-line colorizer**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/IntraLineColorizer.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;
  using GitDelta.Core.Models;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;

  /// <summary>
  /// Applies intra-line (word-level) background tints from IntraSpan ranges.
  /// Added after the syntax transformer so its background layers over syntax
  /// foreground colors (spec §8). Per-visible-line via AvalonEdit virtualization.
  /// </summary>
  public sealed class IntraLineColorizer : DocumentColorizingTransformer
  {
      private DiffDocumentSide? _side;

      public void SetSide(DiffDocumentSide? side)
      {
          _side = side;
      }

      protected override void ColorizeLine(ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document.DocumentLine line)
      {
          DiffDocumentSide? side = _side;
          if (side is null)
          {
              return;
          }

          int rowIndex = line.LineNumber - 1;
          if (rowIndex < 0 || rowIndex >= side.Rows.Count)
          {
              return;
          }

          DiffRow row = side.Rows[rowIndex];
          if (row.IntraSpans.Count == 0)
          {
              return;
          }

          int lineStart = line.Offset;
          int lineLength = line.Length;

          foreach (IntraSpan span in row.IntraSpans)
          {
              int spanStart = span.Start;
              int spanEnd = span.Start + span.Length;

              // Clamp to the actual line bounds (defensive against off-by-one in source data).
              if (spanStart < 0)
              {
                  spanStart = 0;
              }

              if (spanEnd > lineLength)
              {
                  spanEnd = lineLength;
              }

              if (spanEnd <= spanStart)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              System.Windows.Media.Brush tint = span.Kind == IntraSpanKind.Added
                  ? DiffBrushes.AddedSpan
                  : DiffBrushes.DeletedSpan;

              ChangeLinePart(
                  lineStart + spanStart,
                  lineStart + spanEnd,
                  element => element.TextRunProperties.SetBackgroundBrush(tint));
          }
      }
  }
  ```

  ```powershell

  ```

  ```powershell
  ChangeBarMargin draws the green/red/orange gutter stripe per line.
  IntraLineColorizer applies word-level IntraSpan tints via a
  DocumentColorizingTransformer, layered over syntax foreground colors.
  ```

### Task 7.7: Wire renderers into DiffView; read-only editor setup; binary/truncated fallbacks; display options

**Files:**
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`

Now connect the pieces from 7.3–7.6 into the control: configure each editor read-only with undo disabled, attach the background renderer / change-bar margin / intra-line colorizer per editor, build documents on `FileDiff`/`ViewMode` change, toggle split vs unified visibility, apply binary/truncated overlays, and honor `ShowWhitespace`/`WordWrap`/`TabSize`. Manual verification.

- [ ] **Step 1: Add per-editor render attachment helper + fields**

  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`. Add these usings at the top:

  ```csharp
  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Editing;
  ```

  Add private renderer fields and a configuration method inside the class (replace the placeholder `LeftEditorRef`/`RightEditorRef`/`UnifiedEditorRef` properties from Task 7.2 — they are no longer needed):

  ```csharp
      // One renderer/margin/colorizer per editor surface.
      private readonly DiffLineBackgroundRenderer _leftBg = new();
      private readonly DiffLineBackgroundRenderer _rightBg = new();
      private readonly DiffLineBackgroundRenderer _unifiedBg = new();

      private readonly ChangeBarMargin _leftBar = new();
      private readonly ChangeBarMargin _rightBar = new();
      private readonly ChangeBarMargin _unifiedBar = new();

      private readonly IntraLineColorizer _leftIntra = new();
      private readonly IntraLineColorizer _rightIntra = new();
      private readonly IntraLineColorizer _unifiedIntra = new();

      private bool _editorsConfigured;

      private void ConfigureEditorsOnce()
      {
          if (_editorsConfigured)
          {
              return;
          }

          ConfigureEditor(LeftEditor, _leftBg, _leftBar, _leftIntra);
          ConfigureEditor(RightEditor, _rightBg, _rightBar, _rightIntra);
          ConfigureEditor(UnifiedEditor, _unifiedBg, _unifiedBar, _unifiedIntra);
          _editorsConfigured = true;
      }

      private void ConfigureEditor(
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor,
          DiffLineBackgroundRenderer bg,
          ChangeBarMargin bar,
          IntraLineColorizer intra)
      {
          // Read-only, no undo/edit subsystem cost (spec §8).
          editor.IsReadOnly = true;
          editor.Document = new TextDocument();
          editor.Document.UndoStack.SizeLimit = 0;
          editor.Options.EnableHyperlinks = false;
          editor.Options.EnableEmailHyperlinks = false;
          editor.Options.AllowScrollBelowDocument = false;

          editor.TextArea.TextView.BackgroundRenderers.Add(bg);
          editor.TextArea.LeftMargins.Insert(0, bar);
          editor.TextArea.TextView.LineTransformers.Add(intra); // intra last for now; syntax inserts before it in Phase 8
      }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the render pipeline (document build + mode toggle + fallbacks)**

  Add the rendering methods and replace the empty `OnRenderInputChanged` / `OnDisplayOptionChanged` callbacks:

  ```csharp
      private static void OnRenderInputChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)
      {
          ((DiffView)d).Rebuild();
      }

      private static void OnDisplayOptionChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)
      {
          ((DiffView)d).ApplyDisplayOptions();
      }

      private void Rebuild()
      {
          ConfigureEditorsOnce();
          FileDiff? diff = FileDiff;

          if (diff is null)
          {
              ShowOverlay(EmptyState, null);
              return;
          }

          if (diff.IsBinary)
          {
              ShowOverlay(PlaceholderState, "Binary file — no textual diff");
              return;
          }

          // Real content: hide overlays, build documents.
          EmptyState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
          PlaceholderState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;

          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, ViewMode);

          if (ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified)
          {
              SplitRoot.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
              UnifiedEditor.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
              LoadSide(UnifiedEditor, _unifiedBg, _unifiedBar, _unifiedIntra, model.Unified);
          }
          else
          {
              UnifiedEditor.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
              SplitRoot.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
              LoadSide(LeftEditor, _leftBg, _leftBar, _leftIntra, model.Left);
              LoadSide(RightEditor, _rightBg, _rightBar, _rightIntra, model.Right);
          }

          ApplyDisplayOptions();

          if (diff.IsTruncated)
          {
              // Show overlay text but keep the (partial) diff visible behind it as a banner.
              PlaceholderState.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
              PlaceholderState.VerticalAlignment = VerticalAlignment.Bottom;
              PlaceholderState.Text = "Diff truncated — file too large to show in full";
          }
      }

      private void LoadSide(
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor,
          DiffLineBackgroundRenderer bg,
          ChangeBarMargin bar,
          IntraLineColorizer intra,
          DiffDocumentSide? side)
      {
          editor.Document.Text = side?.Text ?? string.Empty;
          bg.SetSide(side);
          bar.SetSide(side);
          intra.SetSide(side);
          editor.TextArea.TextView.Redraw();
      }

      private void ShowOverlay(System.Windows.Controls.TextBlock overlay, string? text)
      {
          SplitRoot.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
          UnifiedEditor.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
          EmptyState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
          PlaceholderState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;

          overlay.VerticalAlignment = VerticalAlignment.Center;
          if (text is not null)
          {
              overlay.Text = text;
          }

          overlay.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
      }

      private void ApplyDisplayOptions()
      {
          ConfigureEditorsOnce();
          bool wrap = WordWrap && ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified; // word-wrap disabled in split (spec §8)
          foreach (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor in new[] { LeftEditor, RightEditor, UnifiedEditor })
          {
              editor.WordWrap = wrap;
              editor.Options.ShowSpaces = ShowWhitespace;
              editor.Options.ShowTabs = ShowWhitespace;
              editor.Options.IndentationSize = TabSize < 1 ? 4 : TabSize;
          }
      }
  ```


### Task 7.8: Side-by-side scroll synchronization with re-entrancy guard

**Files:**
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`

Per spec §8 / BACKBONE: in split mode the two `TextView.ScrollOffset`s are mirrored both ways, guarded against the feedback loop that mutual scroll handlers would otherwise create. Manual verification.

- [ ] **Step 1: Add the guarded scroll-sync wiring**

  In `ConfigureEditorsOnce` (Task 7.7), after the three `ConfigureEditor` calls, hook the two split editors' scroll events. Add a guard field and the handlers to `DiffView.xaml.cs`:

  ```csharp
      private bool _syncingScroll;

      private void HookSplitScrollSync()
      {
          LeftEditor.TextArea.TextView.ScrollOffsetChanged += (_, _) =>
              MirrorScroll(LeftEditor, RightEditor);
          RightEditor.TextArea.TextView.ScrollOffsetChanged += (_, _) =>
              MirrorScroll(RightEditor, LeftEditor);
      }

      private void MirrorScroll(
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor source,
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor target)
      {
          if (_syncingScroll || ViewMode != DiffViewMode.SideBySide)
          {
              return;
          }

          _syncingScroll = true;
          try
          {
              System.Windows.Vector offset = source.TextArea.TextView.ScrollOffset;
              target.ScrollToVerticalOffset(offset.Y);
              target.ScrollToHorizontalOffset(offset.X);
          }
          finally
          {
              _syncingScroll = false;
          }
      }
  ```

  Then add the hook call at the end of `ConfigureEditorsOnce`:

  ```csharp
          HookSplitScrollSync();
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Build**

  ```powershell
  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj
  ```

  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Manual verification**

  Re-add the temporary harness from Task 7.7 Step 4 but feed a larger `FileDiff` (duplicate the hunk lines ~60 times so the document overflows the viewport). Run:

  ```powershell
  dotnet run --project src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj
  ```

  **Observe:** scrolling the left editor (wheel or scrollbar) moves the right editor in lockstep, and vice versa, both vertically and horizontally. There is no visible jitter/oscillation (the re-entrancy guard prevents the feedback loop). Remove the harness afterward.

- [ ] **Step 4: Commit**

  ```powershell
  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs
  git commit -m @'
  feat(ui): mirror side-by-side scroll with re-entrancy guard

  Hooks both split editors ScrollOffsetChanged, mirroring vertical and
  horizontal offsets; a _syncingScroll flag prevents the feedback loop.

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
  ```

### Task 7.9: Next/prev change navigation + find panel + copy

**Files:**
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`

Implement the four BACKBONE public methods for real: `GoToNextChange`/`GoToPreviousChange` jump the caret/scroll to the next changed (non-context, non-filler) row in the active editor; `ShowFind` opens AvalonEdit's built-in `SearchPanel`; `CopySelection` copies the active editor's selection. Manual verification.

- [ ] **Step 1: Add a helper for the active editor and its side, plus install the search panel**

  In `ConfigureEditor` (Task 7.7), install the search panel per editor. Add to the end of `ConfigureEditor`:

  ```csharp
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchPanel.Install(editor.TextArea);
  ```

  Add this active-editor resolver to `DiffView.xaml.cs`:

  ```csharp
      private ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor ActiveEditor =>
          ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified ? UnifiedEditor : RightEditor;

      private DiffDocumentSide? ActiveSide =>
          ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified
              ? (FileDiff is null ? null : DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(FileDiff, DiffViewMode.Unified).Unified)
              : (FileDiff is null ? null : DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(FileDiff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide).Right);
  ```

  > Note: rebuilding here is cheap (the model is small and already cached conceptually); if profiling shows cost, store the last `DiffDocumentModel` from `Rebuild`. For correctness this is sufficient.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the four public methods (replace the Task 7.2 stubs)**

  ```csharp
      public void GoToNextChange()
      {
          NavigateChange(forward: true);
      }

      public void GoToPreviousChange()
      {
          NavigateChange(forward: false);
      }

      public void ShowFind()
      {
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchPanel.Install(ActiveEditor.TextArea);
          ActiveEditor.Focus();
          // Opens the find panel; AvalonEdit binds Ctrl+F, but we surface it programmatically too.
          ActiveEditor.TextArea.DefaultInputHandler.NestedInputHandlers
              .OfType<ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchInputHandler>()
              .FirstOrDefault()?
              .CommandBindings
              .OfType<System.Windows.Input.CommandBinding>()
              .FirstOrDefault(b => b.Command == ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find);
          // Simpler reliable path: route the Find routed command at the editor.
          if (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.CanExecute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea))
          {
              ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.Execute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea);
          }
      }

      public void CopySelection()
      {
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor = ActiveEditor;
          if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(editor.SelectedText))
          {
              editor.Copy();
          }
      }

      private void NavigateChange(bool forward)
      {
          DiffDocumentSide? side = ActiveSide;
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor = ActiveEditor;
          if (side is null || side.Rows.Count == 0)
          {
              return;
          }

          int currentRow = editor.TextArea.Caret.Line - 1; // 0-based row index
          int count = side.Rows.Count;
          int step = forward ? 1 : -1;

          for (int n = 1; n <= count; n++)
          {
              int idx = currentRow + (step * n);
              if (idx < 0 || idx >= count)
              {
                  break;
              }

              DiffRowKind kind = side.Rows[idx].Kind;
              if (kind is DiffRowKind.Added or DiffRowKind.Deleted or DiffRowKind.Modified)
              {
                  int docLine = idx + 1;
                  editor.ScrollToLine(docLine);
                  editor.TextArea.Caret.Line = docLine;
                  editor.TextArea.Caret.Column = 1;
                  editor.TextArea.Caret.BringCaretToView();
                  return;
              }
          }
      }
  ```

  > Note: `ShowFind`'s dead reflective lookup above is illustrative of the wrong path — keep ONLY the reliable `ApplicationCommands.Find.Execute` block. Delete the `NestedInputHandlers` lines so the method body is just: `SearchPanel.Install`, `Focus`, and the `Find.Execute` guard.

- [ ] **Step 3: Clean up ShowFind to the reliable form**

  Replace `ShowFind` with the final, minimal version:

  ```csharp
      public void ShowFind()
      {
          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchPanel.Install(ActiveEditor.TextArea);
          ActiveEditor.Focus();
          if (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.CanExecute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea))
          {
              ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.Execute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea);
          }
      }
  ```

  Add the needed using at the top of the file:

  ```csharp
  using System.Linq;
  ```

  ```powershell

  ```

  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.

## Phase 8: UI — TextMate Syntax Adapter & Theming

This phase adds syntax highlighting via a hand-written TextMate→AvalonEdit adapter (spec §8: "no maintained bridge exists, so we own it"), selected by `SyntaxLanguageId`, with DarkPlus/LightPlus chosen by `IsDarkTheme` and re-applied on theme change, a language-id-from-extension map, and a large/binary guard that skips tokenization. The language-id map and the guard are **pure logic — unit-tested (TDD)**; the tokenizing transformer and theme wiring are **rendering — manual verification**.

  ```csharp
  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;
  using Shouldly;
  using Xunit;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.Controls;

  public sealed class LanguageIdMapTests
  {
      [Theory]
      [InlineData("Program.cs", "csharp")]
      [InlineData("app.ts", "typescript")]
      [InlineData("index.tsx", "typescriptreact")]
      [InlineData("main.js", "javascript")]
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement the map**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/LanguageIdMap.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using System.IO;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;

  /// <summary>
  /// Maps a file path to a TextMate language id used to select a grammar.
  /// Returns null when no known grammar applies (caller skips highlighting).
  /// </summary>
  public static class LanguageIdMap
  {
      private static readonly IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> ByExtension =
          new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
          {
              [".cs"] = "csharp",
              [".csx"] = "csharp",
              [".ts"] = "typescript",
              [".tsx"] = "typescriptreact",
              [".js"] = "javascript",
              [".jsx"] = "javascriptreact",
              [".mjs"] = "javascript",
              [".cjs"] = "javascript",
              [".json"] = "json",
              [".jsonc"] = "json",
              [".md"] = "markdown",
              [".markdown"] = "markdown",
              [".css"] = "css",
              [".scss"] = "scss",
              [".less"] = "less",
              [".html"] = "html",
              [".htm"] = "html",
              [".xml"] = "xml",
              [".xaml"] = "xml",
              [".ps1"] = "powershell",
              [".psm1"] = "powershell",
              [".yml"] = "yaml",
              [".yaml"] = "yaml",
              [".py"] = "python",
              [".go"] = "go",
              [".rs"] = "rust",
              [".java"] = "java",
              [".c"] = "c",
              [".h"] = "cpp",
              [".cpp"] = "cpp",
              [".hpp"] = "cpp",
              [".sql"] = "sql",
              [".sh"] = "shellscript",
              [".bash"] = "shellscript",
              [".toml"] = "toml",
              [".ini"] = "ini",
          };

      private static readonly IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> ByFileName =
          new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
          {
              ["Dockerfile"] = "dockerfile",
              [".gitignore"] = "ignore",
              [".gitattributes"] = "ignore",
          };

      public static string? FromPath(string? path)
      {
          if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(path))
          {
              return null;
          }

          string fileName = Path.GetFileName(path);
          if (ByFileName.TryGetValue(fileName, out string? byName))
          {
              return byName;
          }

          string ext = Path.GetExtension(path);
          if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(ext) && ByExtension.TryGetValue(ext, out string? byExt))
          {
              return byExt;
          }

          return null;
      }
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests — expect green**


  Expected: `Passed! - Failed: 0, Passed: 15`.

  ```powershell
  feat(ui): add TextMateSharp packages and language-id map

  References TextMateSharp + .Grammars. LanguageIdMap.FromPath resolves a
  TextMate grammar id from a file extension/name (case-insensitive), returning
  null when no grammar applies. Fully unit-tested.
  ```

### Task 8.2: Tokenization guard (size/line threshold) (TDD)

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/SyntaxGuard.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/SyntaxGuardTests.cs`

Spec §8: "A size/line threshold falls back to monochrome (skip tokenization)." This decision is pure logic — TDD it. The guard decides whether to tokenize at all, given the document, a language id, and binary/truncated flags.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/SyntaxGuardTests.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;
  using Shouldly;
  using Xunit;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.Controls;

  public sealed class SyntaxGuardTests
  {
      [Fact]
      public void Allows_small_text_with_a_language()
      {
          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", lineCount: 100, totalChars: 5_000, isBinary: false)
              .ShouldBeTrue();
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Skips_when_no_language_id()
      {
          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize(null, lineCount: 10, totalChars: 200, isBinary: false)
              .ShouldBeFalse();
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Skips_when_binary()
      {
          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", lineCount: 10, totalChars: 200, isBinary: true)
              .ShouldBeFalse();
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Skips_when_too_many_lines()
      {
          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", lineCount: SyntaxGuard.MaxLines + 1, totalChars: 1_000, isBinary: false)
              .ShouldBeFalse();
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Skips_when_too_many_chars()
      {
          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", lineCount: 10, totalChars: SyntaxGuard.MaxChars + 1, isBinary: false)
              .ShouldBeFalse();
      }

      [Fact]
      public void Allows_exactly_at_the_limits()
      {
          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", lineCount: SyntaxGuard.MaxLines, totalChars: SyntaxGuard.MaxChars, isBinary: false)
              .ShouldBeTrue();
      }
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 1 (run): Watch it fail**

  ```powershell
  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~SyntaxGuardTests"
  ```

  Expected: **build error** — `SyntaxGuard` does not exist (`CS0103`).

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the guard**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/SyntaxGuard.cs`:

  ```csharp
  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;

  /// <summary>
  /// Decides whether syntax tokenization should run for a document. Large or binary
  /// content falls back to monochrome (spec §8 performance valve).
  /// </summary>
  public static class SyntaxGuard
  {
      public const int MaxLines = 20_000;
      public const int MaxChars = 2_000_000;

      public static bool ShouldTokenize(string? languageId, int lineCount, int totalChars, bool isBinary)
      {
          if (isBinary || string.IsNullOrEmpty(languageId))
          {
              return false;
          }

          if (lineCount > MaxLines || totalChars > MaxChars)
          {
              return false;
          }

          return true;
      }
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3: Run — expect green**

  ```powershell
  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~SyntaxGuardTests"
  ```

  Expected: `Passed! - Failed: 0, Passed: 6`.

- [ ] **Step 4: Commit**

  ```powershell
  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/SyntaxGuard.cs tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/SyntaxGuardTests.cs
  git commit -m @'
  feat(ui): add tokenization size/binary guard

  SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize skips highlighting when there is no language id,
  the content is binary, or the document exceeds line/char limits (monochrome
  fallback, spec §8). Fully unit-tested.

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
  '@
  ''@
  ```

### Task 8.3: TextMate registry/theme provider

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateThemeProvider.cs`

A small wrapper around TextMateSharp's `RegistryOptions`/`Registry` that exposes a grammar for a language id and the DarkPlus/LightPlus theme chosen by `IsDarkTheme`, plus a way to map a TextMate theme color (hex string) to a frozen WPF `Brush`. The tokenizing transformer (8.4) consumes this. Manual/build verification (it touches the TextMateSharp object model, not rendering).

- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the provider**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateThemeProvider.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using System.Collections.Concurrent;
  using System.Windows.Media;
  using TextMateSharp.Grammars;
  using TextMateSharp.Registry;
  using TextMateSharp.Themes;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;

  /// <summary>
  /// Wraps the TextMateSharp Registry: resolves a grammar by language id and the
  /// DarkPlus/LightPlus theme by IsDarkTheme, and converts theme colors to frozen
  /// WPF brushes (cached). Recreated when the theme changes.
  /// </summary>
  public sealed class TextMateThemeProvider
  {
      private readonly RegistryOptions _options;
      private readonly Registry _registry;
      private readonly Theme _theme;
      private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<int, Brush> _brushCache = new();
      private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, Brush> _hexCache = new();

      public TextMateThemeProvider(bool isDark)
      {
          IsDark = isDark;
          _options = new RegistryOptions(isDark ? ThemeName.DarkPlus : ThemeName.LightPlus);
          _registry = new Registry(_options);
          _theme = _registry.GetTheme();
      }

      public bool IsDark { get; }

      public Theme Theme => _theme;

      /// <summary>Returns the grammar scope name for a VS Code language id, or null.</summary>
      public string? GetScopeName(string languageId) => _options.GetScopeByLanguageId(languageId);

      /// <summary>Loads the grammar for a language id, or null if unavailable.</summary>
      public TextMateSharp.Grammars.IGrammar? LoadGrammar(string languageId)
      {
          string? scope = GetScopeName(languageId);
          return scope is null ? null : _registry.LoadGrammar(scope);
      }

      /// <summary>Resolves a TextMate foreground color id to a frozen brush.</summary>
      public Brush BrushForForeground(int foregroundId)
      {
          return _brushCache.GetOrAdd(foregroundId, id =>
          {
              string? hex = _theme.GetColor(id);
              return BrushFromHex(hex);
          });
      }

      private Brush BrushFromHex(string? hex)
      {
          if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(hex))
          {
              return Brushes.Transparent;
          }

          return _hexCache.GetOrAdd(hex, h =>
          {
              try
              {
                  var color = (Color)ColorConverter.ConvertFromString(h);
                  var brush = new SolidColorBrush(color);
                  brush.Freeze();
                  return brush;
              }
              catch (FormatException)
              {
                  return Brushes.Transparent;
              }
          });
      }
  }
  ```

  > Note: TextMateSharp's exact accessor names can drift across versions (`GetScopeByLanguageId`, `Theme.GetColor(int)`, `IGrammar.TokenizeLine`). If a member name does not resolve in the pinned version, open the package's public surface via the IDE's "Go to Definition" on `RegistryOptions`/`Theme` and adjust the three call sites; the shape (registry → grammar → theme color id → hex) is stable.


### Task 8.4: TextMate colorizing transformer (the adapter)

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateColorizer.cs`

This is the core hand-written TextMate→AvalonEdit adapter (spec §15 risk). A `DocumentColorizingTransformer` that, per visible line, calls `IGrammar.TokenizeLine`, maps each token's scopes to a theme foreground color, and applies it as the line part's foreground. It carries grammar state line-to-line so multi-line constructs (block comments, strings) tokenize correctly. Manual verification.

- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the colorizer**

  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateColorizer.cs`:

  ```csharp
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;
  using TextMateSharp.Grammars;

  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;

  /// <summary>
  /// Hand-written TextMate -> AvalonEdit adapter (spec §15). Tokenizes each visible
  /// line with IGrammar.TokenizeLine, threads grammar state line-to-line, and maps
  /// each token's scopes to a theme foreground brush. Added to LineTransformers
  /// BEFORE the intra-line colorizer so diff tints layer over syntax foregrounds.
  /// </summary>
  public sealed class TextMateColorizer : DocumentColorizingTransformer
  {
      private readonly TextMateThemeProvider _provider;
      private readonly IGrammar _grammar;

      // Cache of end-state per document line so re-tokenizing a single visible line
      // can resume from the prior line's state. Index is 1-based line number.
      private readonly Dictionary<int, IStateStack?> _lineStartState = new();

      public TextMateColorizer(TextMateThemeProvider provider, IGrammar grammar)
      {
          _provider = provider;
          _grammar = grammar;
          _lineStartState[1] = null; // first line starts from the null state
      }

      protected override void ColorizeLine(DocumentLine line)
      {
          string text = CurrentContext.Document.GetText(line);
          IStateStack? startState = GetStartState(line);

          ITokenizeLineResult result = _grammar.TokenizeLine(text, startState, TimeSpan.MaxValue);

          // Remember the end state as the next line's start state.
          _lineStartState[line.LineNumber + 1] = result.RuleStack;

          int lineStart = line.Offset;
          foreach (IToken token in result.Tokens)
          {
              int tokenStart = lineStart + Math.Min(token.StartIndex, text.Length);
              int tokenEnd = lineStart + Math.Min(token.EndIndex, text.Length);
              if (tokenEnd <= tokenStart)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              int foreground = ResolveForeground(token.Scopes);
              if (foreground <= 0)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              System.Windows.Media.Brush brush = _provider.BrushForForeground(foreground);
              ChangeLinePart(tokenStart, tokenEnd, el => el.TextRunProperties.SetForegroundBrush(brush));
          }
      }

      private IStateStack? GetStartState(DocumentLine line)
      {
          if (_lineStartState.TryGetValue(line.LineNumber, out IStateStack? state))
          {
              return state;
          }

          // Tokenize all preceding lines once to build the state chain up to this line.
          IStateStack? running = null;
          for (int n = 1; n < line.LineNumber; n++)
          {
              DocumentLine prior = CurrentContext.Document.GetLineByNumber(n);
              string priorText = CurrentContext.Document.GetText(prior);
              ITokenizeLineResult priorResult = _grammar.TokenizeLine(priorText, running, TimeSpan.MaxValue);
              running = priorResult.RuleStack;
              _lineStartState[n + 1] = running;
          }

          return running;
      }

      private int ResolveForeground(IReadOnlyList<string> scopes)
      {
          // Most-specific scope last; ask the theme for its style and take the foreground.
          for (int i = scopes.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
          {
              List<TextMateSharp.Themes.ThemeTrieElementRule> rules =
                  _provider.Theme.Match(new[] { scopes[i] });
              foreach (TextMateSharp.Themes.ThemeTrieElementRule rule in rules)
              {
                  if (rule.foreground > 0)
                  {
                      return rule.foreground;
                  }
              }
          }

          return 0;
      }
  }
  ```

  > Note: TextMateSharp member spellings to confirm against the pinned version: `IStateStack` (older versions use `StackElement`), `IGrammar.TokenizeLine(string, IStateStack?, TimeSpan)`, `ITokenizeLineResult.Tokens`/`.RuleStack`, `IToken.StartIndex`/`.EndIndex`/`.Scopes`, and `Theme.Match(...)` returning rules with a `foreground` int. If any name differs, adjust the call site — the algorithm (resume state → tokenize → most-specific scope → theme foreground → brush) is the stable contract.

  ```powershell
  Hand-written adapter: per visible line, TokenizeLine with threaded grammar
  state, maps most-specific scope to a theme foreground brush, applied as line
  ```
