### Task 8.5: Integrate syntax into DiffView; theme-driven re-tokenize; guard wiring

**Files:**
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`

Wire syntax into the control: when `SyntaxLanguageId`/`IsDarkTheme` change (the `OnSyntaxChanged` callback stubbed in 7.2), rebuild the `TextMateThemeProvider`, load the grammar, and — only if `SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize` passes — insert a `TextMateColorizer` into each editor's `LineTransformers` **before** the existing `IntraLineColorizer`, so diff tints layer over syntax. Re-applied on theme change. Manual verification.

- [ ] **Step 1: Add syntax fields and the install/clear helpers**

  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`. Add usings:

  ```csharp
  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;
  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;
  ```

  Add fields and helpers to the class:

  ```csharp
      private TextMateThemeProvider? _themeProvider;
      private readonly Dictionary<ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor, TextMateColorizer> _syntaxColorizers = new();

      private void ApplySyntax()
      {
          ConfigureEditorsOnce();
          ClearSyntax();

          string? langId = SyntaxLanguageId;
          FileDiff? diff = FileDiff;
          if (langId is null || diff is null || diff.IsBinary)
          {
              return;
          }

          _themeProvider = new TextMateThemeProvider(IsDarkTheme);

          foreach (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor in new[] { LeftEditor, RightEditor, UnifiedEditor })
          {
              int lineCount = editor.Document.LineCount;
              int chars = editor.Document.TextLength;
              if (!SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize(langId, lineCount, chars, diff.IsBinary))
              {
                  continue;
              }

              TextMateSharp.Grammars.IGrammar? grammar = _themeProvider.LoadGrammar(langId);
              if (grammar is null)
              {
                  continue;
              }

              var colorizer = new TextMateColorizer(_themeProvider, grammar);

              // Insert syntax BEFORE the intra-line colorizer so diff tints layer on top.
              IList<IVisualLineTransformer> transformers = editor.TextArea.TextView.LineTransformers;
              int intraIndex = IndexOfIntra(editor, transformers);
              if (intraIndex >= 0)
              {
                  transformers.Insert(intraIndex, colorizer);
              }
              else
              {
                  transformers.Add(colorizer);
              }

              _syntaxColorizers[editor] = colorizer;
              editor.TextArea.TextView.Redraw();
          }
      }

      private int IndexOfIntra(ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor, IList<IVisualLineTransformer> transformers)
      {
          IntraLineColorizer intra = editor == LeftEditor ? _leftIntra
              : editor == RightEditor ? _rightIntra
              : _unifiedIntra;
          return transformers.IndexOf(intra);
      }

      private void ClearSyntax()
      {
          foreach ((ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor, TextMateColorizer colorizer) in _syntaxColorizers)
          {
              editor.TextArea.TextView.LineTransformers.Remove(colorizer);
              editor.TextArea.TextView.Redraw();
          }

          _syntaxColorizers.Clear();
      }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Wire the OnSyntaxChanged callback and re-run syntax after a rebuild**

  Replace the empty `OnSyntaxChanged` (from Task 7.2):

      {

      }
  ```

  And at the very end of `Rebuild` (Task 7.7), after `ApplyDisplayOptions()` and the truncated banner block, re-apply syntax so a new document gets highlighted:

  ```

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing round-trip test.** The store writes to a path under a base directory we inject so the test does not touch the real `%APPDATA%`. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Settings/JsonSettingsStoreTests.cs`:

```csharp
using System.IO;
using GitDelta.Core.Models;
using GitDelta.Core.Settings;
using Shouldly;
using Xunit;

namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Settings;

public sealed class JsonSettingsStoreTests : IDisposable
{
    private readonly string _baseDir;

    public JsonSettingsStoreTests()
    {
        _baseDir = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "GitDeltaTests", Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N"));
        Directory.CreateDirectory(_baseDir);
    }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        try { Directory.Delete(_baseDir, recursive: true); } catch { /* best effort */ }
    }

    [Fact]
    public void Load_WhenFileMissing_ReturnsDefaults()
    {
        var store = new JsonSettingsStore(_baseDir);

        var result = store.Load();

        result.ShouldBe(new AppSettings());
    }

    [Fact]
    public void SaveThenLoad_RoundTripsAllValues()
    {
        var store = new JsonSettingsStore(_baseDir);
        var settings = new AppSettings
        {
            Theme = AppTheme.Dark,
            DefaultDiffView = DiffViewMode.Unified,
            ContextLines = 7,
            TabSize = 2,
            SyntaxHighlighting = false,
            ExternalEditorCommand = "code -g {file}",
            WindowWidth = 1440,
            WindowHeight = 900,
            HistoryPaneWidth = 320,
            FilesPaneWidth = 300,
        };

        store.Save(settings);
        var reloaded = store.Load();

        reloaded.ShouldBe(settings);
    }

    [Fact]
    public void Load_WhenFileCorrupt_ReturnsDefaults()
    {
        var path = Path.Combine(_baseDir, "GitDelta", "settings.json");
        Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.GetDirectoryName(path)!);
        File.WriteAllText(path, "{ this is not valid json ");
        var store = new JsonSettingsStore(_baseDir);

        var result = store.Load();

        result.ShouldBe(new AppSettings());
    }

    [Fact]

    {
        var store = new JsonSettingsStore(_baseDir);

        store.Save(new AppSettings { ContextLines = 5 });

        File.Exists(Path.Combine(_baseDir, "GitDelta", "settings.json")).ShouldBeTrue();
    }
}

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement `JsonSettingsStore`.** It accepts a base directory (defaults to `%APPDATA%`), writes via temp-file-then-rename for crash safety, and returns defaults on missing/corrupt. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Settings/JsonSettingsStore.cs`:

```csharp
using System.IO;
using System.Text.Json;
using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
using GitDelta.Core.Models;

namespace GitDelta.Core.Settings;

public sealed class JsonSettingsStore : ISettingsStore
{
    private static readonly JsonSerializerOptions SerializerOptions = new()
    {
        WriteIndented = true,
        Converters = { new JsonStringEnumConverter() },
    };

    private readonly string _settingsPath;
    private readonly Lock _gate = new();

    /// <summary>Default constructor targets %APPDATA%/GitDelta/settings.json.</summary>
    public JsonSettingsStore()
        : this(Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.ApplicationData))
    {
    }

    /// <summary>Test/seam constructor: <paramref name="baseDirectory"/> stands in for %APPDATA%.</summary>
    public JsonSettingsStore(string baseDirectory)
    {
        _settingsPath = Path.Combine(baseDirectory, "GitDelta", "settings.json");
    }

    public AppSettings Load()
    {
        lock (_gate)
        {
            if (!File.Exists(_settingsPath))
            {
                return new AppSettings();
            }

            try
            {
                var json = File.ReadAllText(_settingsPath);
                return JsonSerializer.Deserialize<AppSettings>(json, SerializerOptions) ?? new AppSettings();
            }
            catch (Exception ex) when (ex is JsonException or IOException or UnauthorizedAccessException)
            {
                return new AppSettings();
            }
        }
    }

    public void Save(AppSettings settings)
    {
        lock (_gate)
        {
            var directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(_settingsPath)!;
            Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);

            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(settings, SerializerOptions);
            var tempPath = _settingsPath + ".tmp";
            File.WriteAllText(tempPath, json);
            File.Move(tempPath, _settingsPath, overwrite: true);
        }
    }
}
```

```powershell

```

Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 4`.

### Task 9.2: Relative-date formatter for CommitRowViewModel (pure logic, TDD)

`CommitRowViewModel.RelativeDate` needs a deterministic, testable formatter ("2 hours ago", "3 days ago", etc.). We extract it into a WPF-free static helper in Core so it can be unit-tested without instantiating a ViewModel, then have `CommitRowViewModel` call it.

**Files:**

namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Models;

public sealed class RelativeTimeTests

    private static readonly DateTimeOffset Now = new(2026, 5, 29, 12, 0, 0, TimeSpan.Zero);

    [Theory]
    [InlineData(5, "just now")]            // 5 seconds ago
    [InlineData(45, "just now")]           // < 1 minute
    [InlineData(60, "1 minute ago")]
    [InlineData(150, "2 minutes ago")]
    [InlineData(3600, "1 hour ago")]
    [InlineData(7200, "2 hours ago")]
    [InlineData(86400, "yesterday")]
    [InlineData(172800, "2 days ago")]
    [InlineData(604800, "last week")]

        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe(expected);

    {
        var when = Now.AddDays(-70);

        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe("2 months ago");
    }

    [Fact]

    {
        var when = Now.AddDays(-800);

        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe("2 years ago");
    }

    [Fact]

    {
        var when = Now.AddSeconds(30);

        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe("just now");
    }

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement `RelativeTime`.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Models/RelativeTime.cs`:

```csharp
namespace GitDelta.Core.Models;

/// <summary>WPF-free relative-time phrasing used by commit rows.</summary>
public static class RelativeTime
{
    public static string Format(DateTimeOffset when) => Format(when, DateTimeOffset.Now);

    public static string Format(DateTimeOffset when, DateTimeOffset now)
    {
        var delta = now - when;
        if (delta < TimeSpan.Zero)
        {
            delta = TimeSpan.Zero;
        }

        var seconds = delta.TotalSeconds;
        if (seconds < 60)
        {
            return "just now";
        }

        var minutes = (int)(delta.TotalMinutes);
        if (minutes < 60)
        {
            return minutes == 1 ? "1 minute ago" : $"{minutes} minutes ago";
        }

        var hours = (int)(delta.TotalHours);
        if (hours < 24)
        {
            return hours == 1 ? "1 hour ago" : $"{hours} hours ago";
        }

        var days = (int)(delta.TotalDays);
        if (days < 7)
        {
            return days == 1 ? "yesterday" : $"{days} days ago";
        }

        if (days < 30)
        {
            var weeks = days / 7;
            return weeks == 1 ? "last week" : $"{weeks} weeks ago";
        }

        if (days < 365)
        {
            var months = days / 30;
            return months == 1 ? "last month" : $"{months} months ago";
        }

        var years = days / 365;
        return years == 1 ? "last year" : $"{years} years ago";
    }
}
```

```powershell

```

Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 13`.

- [ ] **Step 5: Wire `CommitRowViewModel.RelativeDate` to `RelativeTime`.** Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModel.cs` and ensure the `RelativeDate` property delegates to the formatter. The relevant region of the constructor body should read:

```csharp

```

### Task 9.3: IFolderPicker abstraction + WPF-UI implementation

`ShellViewModel`/`StartViewModel` need to open a folder picker. To keep the ViewModels unit-testable (no live dialogs), define an `IFolderPicker` abstraction. The interface lives in the UI layer (it is a UI concern), and the concrete implementation uses WPF-UI's `Wpf.Ui.Controls.OpenFolderDialog`. ViewModels receive `IFolderPicker` by constructor injection (this matches the `...` parameters in the `ShellViewModel`/`StartViewModel`/`MainWindowViewModel` backbone signatures).

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IFolderPicker.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/WpfFolderPicker.cs`

This is non-unit-testable UI glue (it shows an OS dialog), so we verify by build only; the picker is exercised manually in Task 9.9.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the interface.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IFolderPicker.cs`:

```csharp
namespace GitDelta.UI.Services;

/// <summary>Abstracts the OS "open folder" dialog so ViewModels stay unit-testable.</summary>
public interface IFolderPicker
{
    /// <summary>Shows a folder picker. Returns the selected absolute path, or null if cancelled.</summary>
    string? PickFolder(string title);
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Create the WPF-UI implementation.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/WpfFolderPicker.cs`:

```csharp
using Wpf.Ui.Controls;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Services;

public sealed class WpfFolderPicker : IFolderPicker
{
    public string? PickFolder(string title)
    {
        var dialog = new OpenFolderDialog
        {
            Title = title,
            Multiselect = false,
        };

        if (dialog.ShowDialog() == true && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(dialog.FolderName))
        {
            return dialog.FolderName;
        }

        return null;
    }
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Build to confirm the WPF-UI `OpenFolderDialog` API matches.**

```powershell
dotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj
```

Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. If `OpenFolderDialog` is not found, confirm the WPF-UI package version in `Directory.Packages.props` is the one referenced in Phase 1; `Wpf.Ui.Controls.OpenFolderDialog` is present in WPF-UI 3.x.

### Task 9.4: Value converters for the changed-files list and commit rows

The middle pane needs converters to turn a `ChangeKind` into a status glyph + brush, and to render `+N/-M` counts. These are tiny `IValueConverter`s used from XAML.

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/ChangeKindToBrushConverter.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/BoolToVisibilityConverter.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/NullToVisibilityConverter.cs`

These are UI-only; verify by build. (Glyph/counts text comes from `FileRowViewModel.StatusGlyph`/`Added`/`Deleted`, which were built in an earlier phase.)

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the change-kind brush converter.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/ChangeKindToBrushConverter.cs`:

```csharp
using System.Globalization;
using System.Windows.Data;
using System.Windows.Media;
using GitDelta.Core.Models;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Converters;

/// <summary>Maps a ChangeKind to a status-glyph brush (green add / red delete / orange modify / blue rename).</summary>
public sealed class ChangeKindToBrushConverter : IValueConverter
{
    public object Convert(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)
    {
        var color = value is ChangeKind kind
            ? kind switch
            {
                ChangeKind.Added or ChangeKind.Untracked or ChangeKind.Copied => Color.FromRgb(0x3F, 0xB9, 0x50),
                ChangeKind.Deleted => Color.FromRgb(0xE5, 0x53, 0x4B),
                ChangeKind.Renamed => Color.FromRgb(0x4F, 0x9C, 0xF5),
                ChangeKind.Conflicted => Color.FromRgb(0xD2, 0x9A, 0x1F),
                _ => Color.FromRgb(0xCC, 0x8E, 0x35),
            }
            : Color.FromRgb(0x80, 0x80, 0x80);

        return new SolidColorBrush(color);
    }

    public object ConvertBack(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)
        => throw new NotSupportedException();
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Create the bool-to-visibility converter.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/BoolToVisibilityConverter.cs`:

```csharp
using System.Globalization;
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Data;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Converters;

/// <summary>true => Visible, false => Collapsed. Set Invert=true to flip.</summary>
public sealed class BoolToVisibilityConverter : IValueConverter
{
    public bool Invert { get; set; }

    public object Convert(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)
    {
        var flag = value is true;
        if (Invert)
        {
            flag = !flag;
        }

        return flag ? Visibility.Visible : Visibility.Collapsed;
    }

    public object ConvertBack(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)
        => throw new NotSupportedException();
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Create the null-to-visibility converter.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/NullToVisibilityConverter.cs`:

```csharp
using System.Globalization;
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Data;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Converters;

/// <summary>non-null => Visible, null => Collapsed. Set Invert=true to flip.</summary>
public sealed class NullToVisibilityConverter : IValueConverter
{
    public bool Invert { get; set; }

    public object Convert(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)
    {
        var hasValue = value is not null;
        if (Invert)
        {
            hasValue = !hasValue;
        }

        return hasValue ? Visibility.Visible : Visibility.Collapsed;
    }

    public object ConvertBack(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)
        => throw new NotSupportedException();
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Build to confirm the converters compile.**

```

- [ ] **Step 2: Create the code-behind.** It owns the toolbar `Click` handlers (calling `DiffView` public methods), the infinite-scroll handler (calls `LoadMoreHistoryCommand` near the bottom), the multi-select bridge (pushes selection into `ShellViewModel.SelectedCommits` and triggers comparison), and the flat-toggle (clears/sets the folder grouping). Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Views/ShellView.xaml.cs`:

```csharp
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Controls;
using System.Windows.Data;
using GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Views;

public partial class ShellView : UserControl
{
    public ShellView()
    {
        InitializeComponent();
        Loaded += OnLoaded;
    }

    private ShellViewModel? ViewModel => DataContext as ShellViewModel;

    private void OnLoaded(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
    {
        FlatToggle.Checked += OnFlatToggleChanged;
        FlatToggle.Unchecked += OnFlatToggleChanged;
    }

    private void OnFlatToggleChanged(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (Resources["GroupedFiles"] is not CollectionViewSource cvs)
        {
            return;
        }

        cvs.GroupDescriptions.Clear();
        if (FlatToggle.IsChecked != true)
        {
            cvs.GroupDescriptions.Add(new PropertyGroupDescription("Folder"));
        }
    }

    private void HistoryList_SelectionChanged(object sender, SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (ViewModel is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        ViewModel.SelectedCommits.Clear();
        foreach (var item in HistoryList.SelectedItems)
        {
            if (item is CommitRowViewModel row)
            {
                ViewModel.SelectedCommits.Add(row);
            }
        }

        ViewModel.OnHistorySelectionChanged();
    }

    private void HistoryList_ScrollChanged(object sender, ScrollChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        // Trigger paging when within ~3 rows of the bottom and there is more to scroll.
        if (e.VerticalOffset > 0 && e.VerticalOffset >= e.ExtentHeight - e.ViewportHeight - 3
            && ViewModel?.LoadMoreHistoryCommand.CanExecute(null) == true)
        {
            ViewModel.LoadMoreHistoryCommand.Execute(null);
        }
    }

    private void OnFind(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.ShowFind();

    private void OnPreviousChange(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.GoToPreviousChange();

    private void OnNextChange(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.GoToNextChange();

    private void OnCopy(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.CopySelection();
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Add `OnHistorySelectionChanged` to `ShellViewModel`.** The code-behind needs a method to recompute the `DiffSpec` from the current selection (the backbone says: working-tree selected => `WorkingTreeVsHead`; 1 commit => `CommitVsParent`; 2 => `TwoCommits(older,newer)`). Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/ShellViewModel.cs` and add this method (it drives `SetComparisonAsync`):

```csharp
public void OnHistorySelectionChanged()
{
    if (SelectedCommits.Count == 0)
    {
        return;
    }

    WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected = false;

    DiffSpec spec = SelectedCommits.Count == 1
        ? new DiffSpec.CommitVsParent(SelectedCommits[0].Sha)
        : BuildTwoCommitSpec();

    _ = SetComparisonAsync(spec, CancellationToken.None);
}

private DiffSpec BuildTwoCommitSpec()
{
    // History is newest-first; the lower index is the newer commit.
    var first = SelectedCommits[0];
    var second = SelectedCommits[1];
    var firstIndex = History.IndexOf(first);
    var secondIndex = History.IndexOf(second);
    // older = larger index (further down history) => base; newer => target
    return firstIndex > secondIndex
        ? new DiffSpec.TwoCommits(first.Sha, second.Sha)
        : new DiffSpec.TwoCommits(second.Sha, first.Sha);
}
```

Ensure `using GitDelta.Core.Git;` and `using System.Threading;` are present at the top of `ShellViewModel.cs`.

- [ ] **Step 4: Build to confirm the XAML, converters, and `DiffView` DP bindings all resolve.**

```powershell
dotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj
```

Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. If a WPF-UI `SymbolIcon` name (e.g. `BranchCompare24`) is rejected at build, substitute the closest valid `Wpf.Ui.Controls.SymbolRegular` value (the build error names the offending symbol).

          <ui:Button Icon="{ui:SymbolIcon FolderOpen24}" ToolTip="Open folder"
                     Appearance="Transparent" Command="{Binding OpenFolderCommand}" />
          <ui:Button Icon="{ui:SymbolIcon WeatherMoon24}" ToolTip="Toggle theme"
                     Appearance="Transparent" Command="{Binding ToggleThemeCommand}" />
          <ui:Button Icon="{ui:SymbolIcon Settings24}" ToolTip="Settings"
                     Appearance="Transparent" Command="{Binding OpenSettingsCommand}" />
        </StackPanel>
      </ui:TitleBar.TrailingContent>
    </ui:TitleBar>

    <ContentControl Grid.Row="1" Content="{Binding CurrentContent}" />

    <ContentPresenter x:Name="RootContentDialogHost" Grid.Row="1" />
  </Grid>

The title-bar `OpenFolder`/`ToggleTheme`/`OpenSettings` commands resolve against whatever VM is current. Because `StartViewModel` and `ShellViewModel` both expose an `OpenFolderCommand`, and `MainWindowViewModel` exposes the title-bar-level commands, bind these specific buttons to the current shell context. Implement by binding `DataContext` of the `TitleBar.TrailingContent` `StackPanel` to the window's `MainWindowViewModel` — which is already the window `DataContext` — and have `MainWindowViewModel` forward `OpenFolder`/`ToggleTheme`/`OpenSettings` to the active `ShellViewModel` (added in Step 3).

- [ ] **Step 2: Create the MainWindow code-behind.** It registers the dialog host, watches the system theme, sets `DataContext`, persists size on close, and kicks off `InitializeAsync`. - [ ] **Step 3: Add title-bar forwarding + persistence to `MainWindowViewModel`.** Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModel.cs`. Add observable `WindowWidth`/`WindowHeight` (seeded from settings, persisted on change) and the title-bar relay commands that forward to the active `ShellViewModel`:

```csharp
[ObservableProperty]
private double _windowWidth = 1100;

[ObservableProperty]
private double _windowHeight = 720;

public string? RepoName => (CurrentContent as ShellViewModel)?.RepoName;

[RelayCommand]
private async Task OpenFolderAsync()
{
    switch (CurrentContent)
    {
        case ShellViewModel shell:
            await shell.OpenFolderCommand.ExecuteAsync(null);
            break;
        case StartViewModel start:
            await start.OpenFolderCommand.ExecuteAsync(null);
            break;
    }
}

[RelayCommand]
private void ToggleTheme() => (CurrentContent as ShellViewModel)?.ToggleThemeCommand.Execute(null);

[RelayCommand]
private void OpenSettings() => (CurrentContent as ShellViewModel)?.OpenSettingsCommand.Execute(null);

partial void OnCurrentContentChanged(ObservableObject? value) => OnPropertyChanged(nameof(RepoName));

partial void OnWindowWidthChanged(double value) => PersistWindowSize();

partial void OnWindowHeightChanged(double value) => PersistWindowSize();

private void PersistWindowSize()
{
    var current = _settings.Load();
    _settings.Save(current with { WindowWidth = WindowWidth, WindowHeight = WindowHeight });
}
```

Seed `WindowWidth`/`WindowHeight` from `_settings.Load()` in the constructor, where `_settings` is the injected `ISettingsStore`. Ensure `using CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.ComponentModel;`, `using CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.Input;`, and `using GitDelta.Core.Settings;` are present.

- [ ] **Step 4: Implement `ShellViewModel.OpenSettings` + theme + folder picker + persistence.** Open `ShellViewModel.cs` and implement the relay-command bodies (these are the backbone commands `OpenSettings`, `ToggleTheme`, `OpenFolderAsync`). `OpenSettings` shows the `SettingsDialog`; on `Save`, it persists via `ISettingsStore` and re-applies theme + default diff view. Because the dialog and folder picker are UI, inject `IContentDialogService`, `IFolderPicker`, and a `Func<SettingsViewModel>` (these are the `...` constructor params in the backbone). Add:

```csharp
[RelayCommand]
private async Task OpenSettingsAsync()
{
    var current = _settings.Load();
    var vm = _settingsViewModelFactory();
    var presenter = _contentDialogService.GetDialogHost();
    var dialog = new SettingsDialog(presenter, vm);

    var result = await dialog.ShowAsync(CancellationToken.None);
    if (result != ContentDialogResult.Primary)
    {
        return;
    }

    vm.Save();
    var updated = vm.Result;
    _settings.Save(updated);

    ApplyTheme(updated.Theme);
    Diff.ViewMode = updated.DefaultDiffView;
    Diff.TabSize = updated.TabSize;
}

[RelayCommand]
private void ToggleTheme()
{
    var current = _settings.Load();
    var next = current.Theme == AppTheme.Dark ? AppTheme.Light : AppTheme.Dark;
    _settings.Save(current with { Theme = next });
    ApplyTheme(next);
}

[RelayCommand]
private async Task OpenFolderAsync()
{
    var folder = _folderPicker.PickFolder("Open a Git repository");
    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(folder))
    {
        return;
    }

    var root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(folder, CancellationToken.None);
    if (root is not null)
    {
        await LoadRepositoryAsync(root, CancellationToken.None);
    }
    else
    {
        StatusMessage = "That folder is not inside a Git repository.";
    }
}

private void ApplyTheme(AppTheme theme)
{
    switch (theme)
    {
        case AppTheme.Light:
            ApplicationThemeManager.Apply(ApplicationTheme.Light);
            Diff.IsDarkTheme = false;
            break;
        case AppTheme.Dark:
            ApplicationThemeManager.Apply(ApplicationTheme.Dark);
            Diff.IsDarkTheme = true;
            break;
        default:
            ApplicationThemeManager.ApplySystemTheme();
            Diff.IsDarkTheme = ApplicationThemeManager.GetAppTheme() == ApplicationTheme.Dark;
            break;
    }
}
```

Add the fields `_contentDialogService`, `_folderPicker`, `_settingsViewModelFactory` and assign them from new constructor parameters, and add `using GitDelta.UI.Services;`, `using GitDelta.UI.Views;`, `using Wpf.Ui;`, `using Wpf.Ui.Appearance;`, `using Wpf.Ui.Controls;`.

- [ ] **Step 5: Register everything in the UI Autofac module.** Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/AppModule.cs` and add the registrations (mirroring the org module style: services `SingleInstance`, ViewModels `InstancePerDependency`, the window `SingleInstance`):

```csharp
using Autofac;
using GitDelta.Core.Git;
using GitDelta.Core.Diff;
using GitDelta.Core.Settings;
using GitDelta.UI.Services;
using GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;
using GitDelta.UI.Views;
using Wpf.Ui;

namespace GitDelta.UI;

public sealed class AppModule : Module
{
    protected override void Load(ContainerBuilder builder)
    {
        // Core services
        builder.RegisterType<GitProcessRunner>().As<IGitProcessRunner>().SingleInstance();
        builder.RegisterType<CliGitReader>().As<IGitReader>().SingleInstance();
        builder.RegisterType<DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer>().As<IIntraLineDiffer>().SingleInstance();
        builder.RegisterType<JsonSettingsStore>().As<ISettingsStore>().SingleInstance();

        // UI services
        builder.RegisterType<WpfFolderPicker>().As<IFolderPicker>().SingleInstance();
        builder.RegisterType<ContentDialogService>().As<IContentDialogService>().SingleInstance();

        // ViewModels
        builder.RegisterType<ShellViewModel>().AsSelf().InstancePerDependency();
        builder.RegisterType<StartViewModel>().AsSelf().InstancePerDependency();
        builder.RegisterType<SettingsViewModel>().AsSelf().InstancePerDependency();
        builder.RegisterType<MainWindowViewModel>().AsSelf().SingleInstance();

        // Window
        builder.RegisterType<MainWindow>().AsSelf().SingleInstance();
    }
}
```

`MainWindowViewModel` and `StartViewModel`'s `Func<...>` factory parameters are satisfied automatically by Autofac's relationship support (`Func<T>`). `SettingsViewModel` takes `AppSettings current`; resolve it via a registered delegate factory by registering `builder.Register<Func<SettingsViewModel>>(...)` only if Autofac cannot construct `AppSettings` — instead, change `SettingsViewModel`'s injection to accept `ISettingsStore` and load current settings itself (preferred). If keeping the `AppSettings current` ctor, add:

```csharp
builder.Register<SettingsViewModel>(c =>
        new SettingsViewModel(c.Resolve<ISettingsStore>().Load()))
    .AsSelf().InstancePerDependency();
```

- [ ] **Step 6: Add a `MainWindowViewModel` unit test (it is plain logic with `IGitReader` mocked).** This verifies the start-vs-shell routing through `InitializeAsync`. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModelTests.cs`:

```csharp
using GitDelta.Core.Cli;
using GitDelta.Core.Git;
using GitDelta.Core.Models;
using GitDelta.Core.Settings;
using GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;
using NSubstitute;
using Shouldly;
using Xunit;

namespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.ViewModels;

public sealed class MainWindowViewModelTests
{
    private readonly IGitReader _gitReader = Substitute.For<IGitReader>();
    private readonly ISettingsStore _settings = Substitute.For<ISettingsStore>();

    private MainWindowViewModel CreateSut()
    {
        _settings.Load().Returns(new AppSettings());
        return new MainWindowViewModel(
            _gitReader,
            _settings,
            () => new StartViewModel(_gitReader),
            () => CreateShell());
    }

    private ShellViewModel CreateShell() => Substitute.For<ShellViewModel>();

    [Fact]
    public async Task InitializeAsync_PrintHelpOrStartScreen_ShowsStartViewModel()
    {
        var sut = CreateSut();

        await sut.InitializeAsync(new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.ShowStartScreen), CancellationToken.None);

        sut.CurrentContent.ShouldBeOfType<StartViewModel>();
    }

    [Fact]
    public async Task InitializeAsync_OpenRepo_WhenNotARepo_FallsBackToStart()
    {
        _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync("C:/not/a/repo", Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())
            .Returns(Task.FromResult<string?>(null));
        var sut = CreateSut();

        await sut.InitializeAsync(
            new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree, "C:/not/a/repo"),
            CancellationToken.None);

        sut.CurrentContent.ShouldBeOfType<StartViewModel>();
    }

    [Fact]
    public async Task InitializeAsync_OpenRepo_WhenValidRepo_ShowsShellViewModel()
    {
        _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync("C:/repo", Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())
            .Returns(Task.FromResult<string?>("C:/repo"));
        var sut = CreateSut();

        await sut.InitializeAsync(
            new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree, "C:/repo"),
            CancellationToken.None);

        sut.CurrentContent.ShouldBeOfType<ShellViewModel>();
    }
}
```

If `ShellViewModel` cannot be `Substitute.For<>` because it lacks a parameterless/virtual surface, mark its constructor-injected members behind an interface or relax the test to assert `CurrentContent is not StartViewModel`. The key behavior under test is the routing decision, which lives entirely in `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync`.

## Phase 10: UI — CLI / Console Dual-Mode

GitDelta is a `WinExe` (no console window flashes on GUI launch), but must behave like a CLI for `--help`/`--version` and for the `gitdelta <path>` fast-path. This phase implements arg routing in App startup via `ArgRouter.Route`, the `AttachConsole(ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS)` P/Invoke with a `GetFileType`-guarded `CONOUT$` reopen (so redirection/pipes still work), and passing the resolved `LaunchAction` into `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync`.

`ArgRouter.Route` (pure logic) was built and unit-tested in an earlier Core phase per the backbone; this phase consumes it and adds the native console plumbing (P/Invoke; not unit-testable — verified by running the built exe from a terminal).

### Task 10.1: NativeConsole P/Invoke helper

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/NativeConsole.cs`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/ConsoleOutput.cs`

These wrap unmanaged calls; not unit-testable. Verify by build now and by running from a terminal in Task 10.3.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the P/Invoke surface.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/NativeConsole.cs`. It exposes `TryAttachToParentConsole()` which attaches to the parent terminal and, only if stdout is a real char device (a console), reopens `CONOUT$` so writes appear in the terminal — while leaving redirected/piped stdout untouched so `gitdelta --version > out.txt` and `gitdelta --version | findstr` still work.

```csharp
using System.IO;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;
using Microsoft.Win32.SafeHandles;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Cli;

/// <summary>
/// Win32 console plumbing for a WinExe that must emit text to the launching terminal
/// for --help/--version while preserving redirection and pipes.
/// </summary>
internal static partial class NativeConsole
{
    private const int ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS = -1;

    private const uint GENERIC_WRITE = 0x40000000;
    private const uint FILE_SHARE_WRITE = 0x00000002;
    private const uint OPEN_EXISTING = 3;

    private const uint FILE_TYPE_UNKNOWN = 0x0000;
    private const uint FILE_TYPE_CHAR = 0x0002;

    private const int STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE = -11;

    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
    [return: MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.Bool)]
    private static partial bool AttachConsole(int dwProcessId);

    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
    [return: MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.Bool)]
    private static partial bool FreeConsole();

    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
    private static partial nint GetStdHandle(int nStdHandle);

    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
    private static partial uint GetFileType(nint hFile);

    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", EntryPoint = "CreateFileW", SetLastError = true, StringMarshalling = StringMarshalling.Utf16)]
    private static partial SafeFileHandle CreateFile(
        string lpFileName,
        uint dwDesiredAccess,
        uint dwShareMode,
        nint lpSecurityAttributes,
        uint dwCreationDisposition,
        uint dwFlagsAndAttributes,
        nint hTemplateFile);

    /// <summary>
    /// Attaches to the parent console. Returns true if a console is now available
    /// for writing (whether via an attached terminal or via redirection/pipe).
    /// </summary>
    public static bool TryAttachToParentConsole()
    {
        // If stdout is already redirected (file/pipe), the existing stream is valid —
        // we must NOT replace it, or redirection breaks. Detect that first.
        if (IsStdOutRedirected())
        {
            // Still attach so Console.Out flushes to the right place when not redirected,
            // but the redirected handle already routes correctly; nothing more to do.
            AttachConsole(ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS);
            return true;
        }

        if (!AttachConsole(ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS))
        {
            // No parent console (e.g. launched from Explorer): nothing to write to.
            return false;
        }

        return ReopenStdOutToConsole();
    }

    public static void Detach() => FreeConsole();

    private static bool IsStdOutRedirected()
    {
        var handle = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);
        if (handle == nint.Zero || handle == new nint(-1))
        {
            return false;
        }

        var type = GetFileType(handle);
        // A char device is a console; disk/pipe means redirection is in effect.
        return type is not FILE_TYPE_CHAR and not FILE_TYPE_UNKNOWN;
    }

    private static bool ReopenStdOutToConsole()
    {
        var handle = CreateFile(
            "CONOUT$",
            GENERIC_WRITE,
            FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
            nint.Zero,
            OPEN_EXISTING,
            0,
            nint.Zero);

        if (handle.IsInvalid)
        {
            handle.Dispose();
            return false;
        }

        var stream = new FileStream(handle, FileAccess.Write);
        var writer = new StreamWriter(stream, Console.OutputEncoding) { AutoFlush = true };
        Console.SetOut(writer);
        return true;
    }
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Create the help/version text writer.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/ConsoleOutput.cs`:

```csharp
using System.Reflection;

namespace GitDelta.UI.Cli;

/// <summary>Renders --help / --version text to stdout.</summary>
internal static class ConsoleOutput
{
    public static void WriteHelp()
    {
        Console.WriteLine("GitDelta - a read-only Git diff and commit viewer.");
        Console.WriteLine();
        Console.WriteLine("Usage:");
        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta                 Open the repository in the current directory.");
        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta <path>          Open the repository at <path>.");
        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta --help, -h, -?  Show this help.");
        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta --version, -v   Show the version.");
        Console.WriteLine();
        Console.WriteLine("With no repository context, GitDelta opens its start screen.");
    }

    public static void WriteVersion()
    {
        var version = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly()
            .GetCustomAttribute<AssemblyInformationalVersionAttribute>()?.InformationalVersion
            ?? Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetName().Version?.ToString()
            ?? "0.0.0";

        // Trim any build metadata suffix (e.g. "1.2.3+abcdef").
        var plus = version.IndexOf('+');
        if (plus >= 0)
        {
            version = version[..plus];
        }

        Console.WriteLine($"gitdelta {version}");
    }
}
```

```

### Task 10.2: App startup arg routing + LaunchAction handoff

Wire the App bootstrap to compute the `LaunchAction` via `ArgRouter.Route`, handle `PrintHelp`/`PrintVersion` on the console then shut down without showing a window, and for `OpenRepoWorkingTree`/`ShowStartScreen` build the host, resolve `MainWindow`, and pass the action into `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync`.

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs`

These are bootstrap glue (not unit-testable — the routing decision itself is covered by `ArgRouter` tests in Core and the routing-to-content in `MainWindowViewModelTests`). Verify by build + terminal run.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create App.xaml.** It merges the WPF-UI themes/controls dictionaries (matching the org template) and sets no `StartupUri` (we create the window manually). Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`:

```xml
<Application x:Class="GitDelta.UI.App"
             xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"
             xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml"
             xmlns:ui="http://schemas.lepo.co/wpfui/2022/xaml">
  <Application.Resources>
    <ResourceDictionary>
      <ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>
        <ui:ThemesDictionary Theme="Dark" />
        <ui:ControlsDictionary />
      </ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>
    </ResourceDictionary>
  </Application.Resources>
</Application>
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Create App.xaml.cs.** This is the heart of dual-mode. It (a) routes args first; (b) for help/version attaches the console, writes, detaches, and `Shutdown()`s before any window; (c) otherwise builds the IHost (Autofac), installs the global exception handlers (per spec section 10), resolves `MainWindow`, sets its size, and calls `InitializeAsync` with the routed action. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs`:

```csharp
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Threading;
using Autofac;
using Autofac.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using GitDelta.Core.Cli;
using GitDelta.UI.Cli;
using GitDelta.UI.Views;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;

namespace GitDelta.UI;

public partial class App : Application
{
    private IHost? _host;

    protected override void OnStartup(StartupEventArgs e)
    {
        base.OnStartup(e);

        // e.Args already excludes the exe path. cwd is the launching directory.
        var action = ArgRouter.Route(e.Args, Directory.GetCurrentDirectory());

        // Console-only fast paths: write to the parent terminal and exit without a window.
        if (action.Kind is LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp or LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion)
        {
            RunConsoleMode(action);
            Shutdown();
            return;
        }

        InstallGlobalExceptionHandlers();

        _host = Host.CreateDefaultBuilder()
            .UseServiceProviderFactory(new AutofacServiceProviderFactory())
            .ConfigureContainer<ContainerBuilder>(builder => builder.RegisterModule<AppModule>())
            .Build();

        _host.Start();

        var scope = _host.Services.GetRequiredService<ILifetimeScope>();
        var window = scope.Resolve<MainWindow>();
        window.Show();

        // Kick off async initialization (routing to start screen vs working-tree).
        _ = window.ViewModel.InitializeAsync(action, CancellationToken.None);
    }

    private static void RunConsoleMode(LaunchAction action)
    {
        var attached = NativeConsole.TryAttachToParentConsole();

        if (action.Kind == LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp)
        {
            ConsoleOutput.WriteHelp();
        }
        else
        {
            ConsoleOutput.WriteVersion();
        }

        if (attached)
        {
            Console.Out.Flush();
            NativeConsole.Detach();
        }
    }

    private void InstallGlobalExceptionHandlers()
    {
        DispatcherUnhandledException += OnDispatcherUnhandledException;

        AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += (_, args) =>
        {
            // Non-UI fatal path: log via Debug; structured logging added in the logging phase.
            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine($"[FATAL] {args.ExceptionObject}");
        };

        TaskScheduler.UnobservedTaskException += (_, args) =>
        {
            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine($"[UNOBSERVED] {args.Exception}");
            args.SetObserved();
        };
    }

    private void OnDispatcherUnhandledException(object sender, DispatcherUnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)
    {
        System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine($"[UI] {e.Exception}");
        MessageBox.Show(
            $"An unexpected error occurred: {e.Exception.Message}",
            "GitDelta",
            MessageBoxButton.OK,
            MessageBoxImage.Error);
        e.Handled = e.Exception is not (OutOfMemoryException or StackOverflowException);
    }

    protected override async void OnExit(ExitEventArgs e)
    {
        if (_host is not null)
        {
            await _host.StopAsync();
            _host.Dispose();
        }

        base.OnExit(e);
    }
}
```

Add `using System.IO;` if the analyzer flags `Directory`/`File` (ImplicitUsings covers `System.IO` only via the SDK default set for some workloads — include it explicitly to be safe). Ensure the UI csproj from Phase 1 sets `<ApplicationDefinition Include="App.xaml" />` implicitly (default for WPF SDK) so this `App` is the entry point.

- [ ] **Step 3: Confirm `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync` honors all `LaunchActionKind`s.** Open `MainWindowViewModel.cs` and verify `InitializeAsync` matches the routing in the backbone: `ShowStartScreen` => `ShowStartAsync()`; `OpenRepoWorkingTree` => resolve via `IGitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(action.RepoPath!)`, on null fall back to `ShowStartAsync()`, otherwise `OpenRepositoryAsync(root)`. (`PrintHelp`/`PrintVersion` never reach here because App handled them.) If the body is not already present, implement:

```csharp
public async Task InitializeAsync(LaunchAction action, CancellationToken ct)
{
    switch (action.Kind)
    {
        case LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree:
            var root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(action.RepoPath!, ct);
            if (root is not null)
            {
                await OpenRepositoryAsync(root);
            }
            else
            {
                await ShowStartAsync();
            }
            break;

        default:
            await ShowStartAsync();
            break;
    }
}
```

```

## Phase 11: Packaging & Distribution

This phase produces the Release publish configuration for `src/GitDelta.UI`, the Inno Setup installer (`installer/GitDelta.iss`), a README packaging/PATH section, and an end-to-end verification checklist. None of this phase is unit-testable (publish output, installer behavior, README prose), so every task uses **implementation steps with complete code/markup + a manual build/run verification step + a commit**. Verification steps are explicitly manual where noted.

This phase assumes the earlier phases already produced: `GitDelta.sln`, `src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` (WinExe, `net10.0-windows10.0.26100.0`, `UseWPF`, AssemblyName/output exe `gitdelta`), `Directory.Build.props`, `Directory.Packages.props`, `version.json`, and `CLAUDE.md`. This phase only adds publish properties, the installer folder, the runtime bootstrapper bundling, and docs — it does not redefine those projects.

> **Prerequisites for the engineer's machine (one-time, manual):**
> - .NET 10 SDK installed (`dotnet --version` reports `10.x`).
> - Inno Setup 6.x installed (provides the compiler `ISCC.exe`, normally at `C:\Program Files (x86)\Inno Setup 6\ISCC.exe`). Install it from https://jrsoftware.org/isdl.php or via `winget install JRSoftware.InnoSetup`.

### Task 11.1: Add the Release single-file publish configuration to GitDelta.UI

**Files:**
- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/publish.ps1`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/Directory.Build.props.publish.notes.md` *(deleted before commit — scratch only; see Step 4)*

- [ ] **Step 1: Read the current GitDelta.UI.csproj.**
  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` and confirm it already contains `<OutputType>WinExe</OutputType>`, `<UseWPF>true</UseWPF>`, and `<AssemblyName>gitdelta</AssemblyName>` (so the produced exe is `gitdelta.exe`). If `<AssemblyName>gitdelta</AssemblyName>` is missing, that is a Phase 1 contract violation — add it now inside the first `<PropertyGroup>`. The publish properties below depend on the assembly name being `gitdelta`.

- [ ] **Step 2: Add the publish PropertyGroup to GitDelta.UI.csproj.**
  These properties are scoped to `Configuration == Release` so debug builds stay fast and un-bundled. We set framework-dependent single-file (`SelfContained=false`), enable native-lib self-extract and compression, and explicitly turn **off** trimming (WPF trimming is SDK-disabled and would error). `RuntimeIdentifier` is set here so `dotnet build -c Release` and IDE publish both agree; the CLI command in Step 3 also passes `-r win-x64` for clarity.
  Add this block to `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`, immediately before the closing `</Project>` tag:

  ```xml
  <!-- Release single-file publish: framework-dependent (.NET 10 Desktop Runtime required on the
       target machine). No trimming (WPF trimming is disabled by the SDK and would fail the build). -->
  <PropertyGroup Condition="'$(Configuration)' == 'Release'">
    <RuntimeIdentifier>win-x64</RuntimeIdentifier>
    <PlatformTarget>x64</PlatformTarget>
    <SelfContained>false</SelfContained>
    <PublishSingleFile>true</PublishSingleFile>
    <IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract>true</IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract>
    <EnableCompressionInSingleFile>true</EnableCompressionInSingleFile>
    <PublishTrimmed>false</PublishTrimmed>
    <PublishReadyToRun>false</PublishReadyToRun>
    <DebugType>embedded</DebugType>
    <SatelliteResourceLanguages>en</SatelliteResourceLanguages>
  </PropertyGroup>
  ```

  > Note: `IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract=true` makes the single exe self-extract the few unmanaged WPF helper DLLs at first run; without it WPF apps refuse to publish as a true single file. `DebugType=embedded` keeps the PDB inside the exe so we ship one file. `SatelliteResourceLanguages=en` drops localized resource folders (smaller, single-file-friendly).

- [ ] **Step 3: Create the publish helper script.**
  This script centralizes the exact publish command so the installer build (Task 11.2) and humans use the same output path. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/publish.ps1`:

  ```powershell
  #Requires -Version 7.0
  <#
  .SYNOPSIS
    Publishes GitDelta.UI as a framework-dependent, compressed, single-file gitdelta.exe.
  .DESCRIPTION
    Output: <repo>\publish\gitdelta.exe  (plus gitdelta.pdb is embedded, so one file).
    Framework-dependent: the target machine needs the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime (the installer
    in Task 11.2 detects and installs it).
  #>
  [CmdletBinding()]
  param(
      [string] $Configuration = 'Release',
      [string] $Runtime       = 'win-x64'
  )

  $ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'

  $repoRoot   = Split-Path -Parent $PSScriptRoot
  $project    = Join-Path $repoRoot 'src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj'
  $outDir     = Join-Path $repoRoot 'publish'

  if (Test-Path $outDir) {
      Remove-Item -Recurse -Force $outDir
  }

  Write-Host "Publishing GitDelta.UI ($Configuration / $Runtime) -> $outDir" -ForegroundColor Cyan

  dotnet publish $project `
      -c $Configuration `
      -r $Runtime `
      --self-contained false `
      -p:PublishSingleFile=true `
      -p:IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract=true `
      -p:EnableCompressionInSingleFile=true `
      -p:PublishTrimmed=false `
      -o $outDir

  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
      throw "dotnet publish failed with exit code $LASTEXITCODE"
  }

  $exe = Join-Path $outDir 'gitdelta.exe'
  if (-not (Test-Path $exe)) {
      throw "Expected output not found: $exe"
  }

  $sizeMb = [math]::Round((Get-Item $exe).Length / 1MB, 1)
  Write-Host "OK: $exe ($sizeMb MB)" -ForegroundColor Green
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4: Build-verify the publish (MANUAL).**
  Run the exact framework-dependent single-file publish command (this is the canonical command the spec requires). From the repo root `C:/code/projects/GitDelta`:

  ```powershell

  ```

  **Expected:** the command ends with `Build succeeded` / no errors, and `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/publish/gitdelta.exe` exists. Verify the single-file shape and that no trimming was applied:

  ```powershell
  Get-ChildItem C:/code/projects/GitDelta/publish | Select-Object Name, Length
  ```

  **Expected to observe:** `gitdelta.exe` present, size roughly **5–15 MB** (compressed single file). There should be **no** `*.dll` next to it for the managed app assemblies (framework-dependent + single-file bundles them inside the exe). A `gitdelta.exe` plus possibly a couple of `*.json` config files is fine; a folder full of dozens of DLLs means single-file was NOT applied — re-check Step 2.

  Smoke-run the version path against the built exe (this is the same `--version` path Phase 0/CLI implemented):

  ```powershell
  & C:/code/projects/GitDelta/publish/gitdelta.exe --version
  ```

  **Expected:** the version string (e.g. `gitdelta 1.0.0`) prints to the terminal and the process exits without launching a window. Now delete the scratch notes file if you created one and remove the throwaway `publish/` output from source control consideration (it must be gitignored — see Step 5):

  ```

  build: add framework-dependent single-file Release publish for gitdelta.exe

    EnableCompressionInSingleFile / SelfContained=false to Release (no trimming).

### Task 11.2: Author the Inno Setup installer (per-user, PATH, runtime detection)

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/GitDelta.iss`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/runtime/.gitkeep`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/fetch-runtime.ps1`
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1`

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the runtime bundle folder and fetch script.**
  The installer bundles the .NET 10 **Desktop** Runtime offline installer so users without it get a one-click experience. The exe itself is not committed (it is large and license-redistributed via Microsoft's CDN); this script downloads it into `installer/runtime/` before compiling the installer.
  First create the placeholder so the folder exists in git: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/runtime/.gitkeep` with a single line:

  ```text
  Bundled .NET Desktop Runtime installer is fetched here by build/../installer/fetch-runtime.ps1 (gitignored).
  ```

  Then create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/fetch-runtime.ps1`:

  ```powershell
  #Requires -Version 7.0
  <#
  .SYNOPSIS
    Downloads the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime (x64) offline installer into installer/runtime/.
  .DESCRIPTION
    The file is bundled by GitDelta.iss and run silently on the target machine only when the
    runtime is missing. The exe is gitignored (fetched at build time, never committed).
  #>
  [CmdletBinding()]
  param(
      # Pinned to a known .NET 10 Desktop Runtime build. Update when bumping the runtime.
      [string] $Version  = '10.0.0',
      [string] $FileName = 'windowsdesktop-runtime-10.0.0-win-x64.exe'
  )

  $ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'
  $runtimeDir = $PSScriptRoot
  $target     = Join-Path $runtimeDir $FileName

  if (Test-Path $target) {
      Write-Host "Already present: $target" -ForegroundColor Green
      return
  }

  # Microsoft's stable aka.ms redirector for the .NET Desktop Runtime offline installer.
  $url = "https://aka.ms/dotnet/$Version/windowsdesktop-runtime-win-x64.exe"
  Write-Host "Downloading .NET Desktop Runtime $Version -> $target" -ForegroundColor Cyan
  Invoke-WebRequest -Uri $url -OutFile $target -UseBasicParsing

  if (-not (Test-Path $target) -or (Get-Item $target).Length -lt 10MB) {
      throw "Runtime download failed or file too small: $target"
  }
  Write-Host "OK: $target" -ForegroundColor Green
  ```

  > If the pinned `aka.ms` link or filename changes for the final 10.x build, update the `-Version`/`-FileName` defaults here and the `RuntimeInstaller` constant in `GitDelta.iss` (Step 2) to match.

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the full Inno Setup script.**
  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/GitDelta.iss` with the complete script below. It is per-user (`PrivilegesRequired=lowest`), installs to `{localappdata}\Programs\GitDelta`, idempotently appends the install dir to `HKCU\Environment\Path` as `REG_EXPAND_SZ` via Pascal scripting (never `setx`), removes that PATH entry on uninstall, creates a Start Menu shortcut, gets an automatic Add/Remove Programs entry, and detects the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime — running the bundled silent installer if missing, or opening the download page if the bundle is absent.

  ```ini
  ; GitDelta installer (Inno Setup 6.x)
  ; Per-user, no admin. Installs gitdelta.exe to %LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta,
  ; puts the install dir on the per-user PATH, and ensures the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime.

  #define AppName        "GitDelta"
  #define AppExeName     "gitdelta.exe"
  #define AppPublisher   "Morten Brudvik"
  #define AppUrl         "https://github.com/mortenbrudvik/GitDelta"
  #define AppVersion     "1.0.0"
  ; The exe produced by build/publish.ps1
  #define PublishDir     "..\publish"
  ; Bundled .NET Desktop Runtime installer (fetched by installer\fetch-runtime.ps1).
  #define RuntimeInstaller "windowsdesktop-runtime-10.0.0-win-x64.exe"
  #define RuntimeDownloadUrl "https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet/10.0/runtime"

  [Setup]
  AppId={{6D2B6F2E-7C2C-4F4E-9D3B-7A2E2C9A1F10}
  AppName={#AppName}
  AppVersion={#AppVersion}
  AppPublisher={#AppPublisher}
  AppPublisherURL={#AppUrl}
  AppSupportURL={#AppUrl}
  AppUpdatesURL={#AppUrl}/releases
  ; Per-user install: no UAC elevation, lands in %LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta.
  PrivilegesRequired=lowest
  PrivilegesRequiredOverridesAllowed=dialog
  DefaultDirName={localappdata}\Programs\{#AppName}
  DisableProgramGroupPage=yes
  DefaultGroupName={#AppName}
  ; Required so Inno broadcasts WM_SETTINGCHANGE after we touch PATH (new terminals pick it up).
  ChangesEnvironment=yes
  ; Per-user uninstaller / Add-Remove-Programs registration (HKCU).
  UninstallDisplayName={#AppName}
  UninstallDisplayIcon={app}\{#AppExeName}
  Compression=lzma2/max
  SolidCompression=yes
  WizardStyle=modern
  ArchitecturesAllowed=x64compatible
  ArchitecturesInstallIn64BitMode=x64compatible
  OutputDir=Output
  OutputBaseFilename=GitDelta-{#AppVersion}-setup
  SetupIconFile=..\src\GitDelta.UI\Assets\gitdelta.ico

  [Languages]
  Name: "english"; MessagesFile: "compiler:Default.isl"

  [Tasks]
  Name: "addtopath"; Description: "Add GitDelta to the PATH (run 'gitdelta' from any terminal)"; GroupDescription: "Integration:"
  Name: "startmenu"; Description: "Create a Start Menu shortcut"; GroupDescription: "Shortcuts:"

  [Files]
  ; The single-file framework-dependent exe.
  Source: "{#PublishDir}\{#AppExeName}"; DestDir: "{app}"; Flags: ignoreversion
  ; Bundle the runtime installer ONLY if it was fetched; runs silently on demand (see [Run]).
  Source: "runtime\{#RuntimeInstaller}"; DestDir: "{tmp}"; Flags: deleteafterinstall external skipifsourcedoesntexist; Check: NeedsDotNetRuntime

  [Icons]
  Name: "{group}\{#AppName}"; Filename: "{app}\{#AppExeName}"; Tasks: startmenu
  Name: "{group}\Uninstall {#AppName}"; Filename: "{uninstallexe}"; Tasks: startmenu

  [Run]
  ; Install the .NET Desktop Runtime silently if missing AND we bundled it.
  Filename: "{tmp}\{#RuntimeInstaller}"; Parameters: "/install /quiet /norestart"; \
      StatusMsg: "Installing the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime..."; \
      Flags: waituntilterminated; Check: ShouldRunBundledRuntime
  ; If the runtime is missing and was NOT bundled, open the download page after install.
  Filename: "{#RuntimeDownloadUrl}"; Description: "Download the required .NET 10 Desktop Runtime"; \
      Flags: shellexec postinstall skipifsilent; Check: NeedsRuntimeButNotBundled

  [Code]
  const
    EnvironmentKey = 'Environment';

  var
    GBundledRuntimePresent: Boolean;

  { ---- PATH helpers (HKCU\Environment, REG_EXPAND_SZ, idempotent, never setx) ---- }

  function GetPathValue(var Value: string): Boolean;
  begin
    Result := RegQueryStringValue(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, EnvironmentKey, 'Path', Value);
    if not Result then
      Value := '';
  end;

  { Returns True if Dir already appears as a whole entry in the ';'-delimited PathList. }
  function PathContainsDir(const PathList, Dir: string): Boolean;
  var
    Hay, Needle: string;
  begin
    Hay    := ';' + Uppercase(Trim(PathList)) + ';';
    Needle := ';' + Uppercase(Trim(Dir)) + ';';
    Result := Pos(Needle, Hay) > 0;
  end;

  procedure AddDirToPath(const Dir: string);
  var
    PathList, NewPath: string;
  begin
    GetPathValue(PathList);
    if PathContainsDir(PathList, Dir) then
      exit; { idempotent: already present, do nothing }

    if (PathList = '') then
      NewPath := Dir
    else if (Copy(PathList, Length(PathList), 1) = ';') then
      NewPath := PathList + Dir
    else
      NewPath := PathList + ';' + Dir;

    { REG_EXPAND_SZ so other entries with %VAR% keep expanding. Inno broadcasts
      WM_SETTINGCHANGE on completion because ChangesEnvironment=yes. }
    RegWriteExpandStringValue(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, EnvironmentKey, 'Path', NewPath);
  end;

  procedure RemoveDirFromPath(const Dir: string);
  var
    PathList, Rebuilt, Part: string;
    P: Integer;
  begin
    if not GetPathValue(PathList) then
      exit;

    Rebuilt := '';
    PathList := PathList + ';';
    repeat
      P := Pos(';', PathList);
      Part := Trim(Copy(PathList, 1, P - 1));
      PathList := Copy(PathList, P + 1, Length(PathList));
      if (Part <> '') and (Uppercase(Part) <> Uppercase(Trim(Dir))) then
      begin
        if Rebuilt = '' then
          Rebuilt := Part
        else
          Rebuilt := Rebuilt + ';' + Part;
      end;
    until PathList = '';

    RegWriteExpandStringValue(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, EnvironmentKey, 'Path', Rebuilt);
  end;

  { ---- .NET 10 Desktop Runtime detection ---- }

  { True if a Microsoft.WindowsDesktop.App 10.x shared framework folder exists. }
  function IsDotNet10DesktopRuntimeInstalled(): Boolean;
  var
    FindRec: TFindRec;
    BaseDir: string;
  begin
    Result := False;
    { Per-machine x64 install location. dotnet.exe also resolves it via PATH, but the
      shared framework folder is the reliable, no-process probe. }
    BaseDir := ExpandConstant('{commonpf64}\dotnet\shared\Microsoft.WindowsDesktop.App');
    if not DirExists(BaseDir) then
      exit;

    if FindFirst(BaseDir + '\10.*', FindRec) then
    try
      repeat
        if (FindRec.Attributes and FILE_ATTRIBUTE_DIRECTORY) <> 0 then
        begin
          Result := True;
          break;
        end;
      until not FindNext(FindRec);
    finally
      FindClose(FindRec);
    end;
  end;

  function NeedsDotNetRuntime(): Boolean;
  begin
    Result := not IsDotNet10DesktopRuntimeInstalled();
  end;

  { True only when the runtime is missing AND the bundled installer made it onto disk. }
  function ShouldRunBundledRuntime(): Boolean;
  begin
    Result := NeedsDotNetRuntime() and GBundledRuntimePresent;
  end;

  { True when the runtime is missing but no bundle was shipped (open download page). }
  function NeedsRuntimeButNotBundled(): Boolean;
  begin
    Result := NeedsDotNetRuntime() and (not GBundledRuntimePresent);
  end;

  { ---- Wizard wiring ---- }

  procedure InitializeWizard();
  begin
    { Record whether the bundle was compiled into this setup (source existed at compile time
      AND extracted to {tmp}). We approximate "shipped" by checking the source file existed;
      the [Files] 'skipifsourcedoesntexist' flag handles the compile-time-absent case. }
    GBundledRuntimePresent := FileExists(ExpandConstant('{tmp}\{#RuntimeInstaller}'));
  end;

  procedure CurStepChanged(CurStep: TSetupStep);
  begin
    if CurStep = ssPostInstall then
    begin
      { Re-evaluate after [Files] extraction so the {tmp} probe is accurate. }
      GBundledRuntimePresent := FileExists(ExpandConstant('{tmp}\{#RuntimeInstaller}'));
      if WizardIsTaskSelected('addtopath') then
        AddDirToPath(ExpandConstant('{app}'));
    end;
  end;

  procedure CurUninstallStepChanged(CurUninstallStep: TUninstallStep);
  begin
    if CurUninstallStep = usUninstall then
      RemoveDirFromPath(ExpandConstant('{app}'));
  end;
  ```

  > Notes for the engineer:
  > - The `[Files]` line for the runtime uses `skipifsourcedoesntexist`, so the installer still compiles even when `installer/runtime/` is empty (CI without the bundle). In that case `GBundledRuntimePresent` is false and, if the runtime is missing, the post-install step opens the Microsoft download page.
  > - `RegWriteExpandStringValue` writes `REG_EXPAND_SZ` — the correct PATH type. We never call `setx` (which truncates at 1024 chars).
  > - `ChangesEnvironment=yes` is what makes Inno broadcast `WM_SETTINGCHANGE`, so freshly opened terminals see the new PATH without a logoff.
  > - `SetupIconFile` points at `src/GitDelta.UI/Assets/gitdelta.ico`. If the icon asset does not yet exist from an earlier UI phase, either add a 256x256 `gitdelta.ico` there or temporarily comment out the `SetupIconFile` and `UninstallDisplayIcon` lines to compile — but the icon is expected to exist before release.

- [ ] **Step 3: Create the installer build script.**
  This orchestrates: publish → fetch runtime → compile installer. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1`:

  ```powershell
  #Requires -Version 7.0
  <#
  .SYNOPSIS
    End-to-end installer build: publish gitdelta.exe, fetch the bundled runtime, compile GitDelta.iss.
  .DESCRIPTION
    Output: installer\Output\GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe
  #>
  [CmdletBinding()]
  param(
      [switch] $SkipRuntimeBundle,
      [string] $IsccPath = 'C:\Program Files (x86)\Inno Setup 6\ISCC.exe'
  )

  $ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'
  $repoRoot   = Split-Path -Parent $PSScriptRoot
  $issFile    = Join-Path $repoRoot 'installer/GitDelta.iss'

  # 1) Publish the single-file exe.
  & (Join-Path $PSScriptRoot 'publish.ps1')

  # 2) Fetch the bundled .NET Desktop Runtime (unless skipped, e.g. CI that relies on download page).
  if (-not $SkipRuntimeBundle) {
      & (Join-Path $repoRoot 'installer/fetch-runtime.ps1')
  }
  else {
      Write-Host "Skipping runtime bundle (installer will open the download page if runtime is missing)." -ForegroundColor Yellow
  }

  # 3) Compile the installer.
  if (-not (Test-Path $IsccPath)) {
      throw "Inno Setup compiler not found at '$IsccPath'. Install Inno Setup 6 or pass -IsccPath."
  }
  Write-Host "Compiling installer: $issFile" -ForegroundColor Cyan
  & $IsccPath $issFile
  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
      throw "ISCC.exe failed with exit code $LASTEXITCODE"
  }

  $out = Get-ChildItem (Join-Path $repoRoot 'installer/Output') -Filter '*-setup.exe' |
         Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending | Select-Object -First 1
  Write-Host "OK: $($out.FullName) ($([math]::Round($out.Length/1MB,1)) MB)" -ForegroundColor Green
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4: Compile-verify the installer (MANUAL).**
  This is a manual verification — installer compilation cannot be unit-tested. From the repo root:

  ```powershell
  pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1
  ```

  **Expected:** publish succeeds, the runtime download completes (or is skipped), and `ISCC.exe` prints `Successful compile` ending with the output path. Confirm the artifact:

  ```powershell
  Get-ChildItem C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/Output | Select-Object Name, Length
  ```

  **Expected to observe:** `GitDelta-1.0.0-setup.exe` exists. If you bundled the runtime its size will be large (~50–70 MB); without the bundle (`-SkipRuntimeBundle`) it will be ~5–15 MB. If `ISCC.exe` reports a missing `SetupIconFile`, address the icon per the Step 2 note before continuing.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit.**

  ```powershell
  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add installer/GitDelta.iss installer/runtime/.gitkeep installer/fetch-runtime.ps1 build/make-installer.ps1
  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'
  build: add Inno Setup per-user installer with PATH + .NET runtime detection

  - installer/GitDelta.iss: PrivilegesRequired=lowest, install to
    {localappdata}\Programs\GitDelta, ChangesEnvironment=yes.
  - Idempotent HKCU\Environment\Path append (REG_EXPAND_SZ) via Pascal, removed on
    uninstall; never uses setx.
  - Start Menu shortcut + automatic Add/Remove Programs entry.
  - Detect .NET 10 Desktop Runtime; run bundled silent installer or open download page.

### Task 11.3: Document distribution, SmartScreen, and PATH usage in the README

**Files:**
- Modify (or Create if absent): `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md`

- [ ] **Step 1: Read the existing README (if any).**
  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md`. If it does not exist, create it with the full content in Step 2. If it exists, append the `## Installation` and `## Using the `gitdelta` command` sections from Step 2 after the project intro (do not duplicate an existing title).

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the Installation & usage documentation.**
  Put this content into `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md` (full file shown; if the file already exists, merge the two new `##` sections in rather than overwriting your existing intro):

  ```markdown
  # GitDelta

  GitDelta is a lightweight, native Windows 11 **read-only** Git diff and commit viewer.
  Inspect uncommitted changes, what a single commit introduced, or the diff between any two
  commits — in a modern Fluent UI. It is not a full Git client (no staging, committing, or
  pushing); it only visualizes.

  ## Installation

  GitDelta is distributed as a **per-user installer** via
  [GitHub Releases](https://github.com/mortenbrudvik/GitDelta/releases). Download
  `GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe` and run it. No administrator rights are required — GitDelta
  installs to `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta` for the current user only.

  The installer will:

  - Install `gitdelta.exe`.
  - Add the install folder to your **per-user PATH** so you can run `gitdelta` from any terminal.
  - Create a Start Menu shortcut and an entry in **Settings → Apps → Installed apps** (for clean uninstall).
  - Detect the **.NET 10 Desktop Runtime** and, if it is missing, either install the bundled
    runtime silently or open the Microsoft download page.

  ### "Windows protected your PC" / SmartScreen warning

  GitDelta v1 is **not code-signed**. When you run the installer, Microsoft Defender SmartScreen
  may show **"Windows protected your PC — Unknown publisher"**. This is expected for unsigned
  software and does not indicate a problem with the download.

  To proceed:

  1. Click **More info**.
  2. Click **Run anyway**.

  If you prefer, verify the download first: each GitHub Release lists the SHA-256 checksum of the
  installer. Compare it with:

  ```powershell
  Get-FileHash .\GitDelta-1.0.0-setup.exe -Algorithm SHA256
  ```

  ### Prerequisites

  - **Windows 11** (x64).
  - **.NET 10 Desktop Runtime** — the installer adds it for you if missing.
  - **Git for Windows ≥ 2.30** on your PATH. GitDelta shells out to the `git` CLI; if git is not
    found it shows an actionable screen linking the Git for Windows download. Install via
    `winget install Git.Git` or from https://git-scm.com/download/win.

  ## Using the `gitdelta` command

  After installing (and **opening a new terminal** so the updated PATH takes effect), run:

  | Command | What it does |
  |---|---|
  | `gitdelta` | Opens the repository in the current folder at the **working-tree-vs-HEAD** view. |
  | `gitdelta <path>` | Opens the repository at `<path>` at the working-tree-vs-HEAD view. |
  | `gitdelta` (outside a repo) | Opens the **start screen** with an "Open folder" picker. |
  | `gitdelta --version` | Prints the version to the terminal and exits. |
  | `gitdelta --help` | Prints usage to the terminal and exits. |

  > **New PATH not picked up?** The installer broadcasts a system message so freshly opened
  > terminals see the updated PATH immediately. Terminals that were already open before installing
  > will **not** see `gitdelta` until you open a new one. (Bare `gitdelta` resolves via PATH;
  > `cmd` and PowerShell do not consult Windows "App Paths", which is why the installer edits PATH.)

  ## Uninstalling

  Uninstall from **Settings → Apps → Installed apps → GitDelta → Uninstall**, or via the
  "Uninstall GitDelta" Start Menu shortcut. Uninstalling removes the install folder **and** the
  PATH entry it added.

  ## Building from source

  ```powershell
  # Restore, build (zero warnings — TreatWarningsAsErrors), and test.
  dotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln -c Release
  dotnet test  C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln

  # Produce the single-file gitdelta.exe in .\publish\
  pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/publish.ps1

  # Build the full installer (publish + bundle runtime + compile Inno Setup)
  pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1
  ```

  Building the installer requires [Inno Setup 6](https://jrsoftware.org/isdl.php)
  (`winget install JRSoftware.InnoSetup`).
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3: Verify the README renders (MANUAL).**

  ```powershell

  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

### Task 11.4: End-to-end packaging verification checklist (clean Win11)

**Files:**
- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/docs/release-verification.md`

This task is entirely **manual verification** — there is nothing to unit-test. It produces a repeatable checklist used before publishing each GitHub Release, ideally run on a clean Windows 11 VM (or a freshly-reset user profile) that does **not** already have the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime or `gitdelta` on PATH.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the release verification checklist.**
  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/docs/release-verification.md`:

  ```markdown
  # GitDelta — Release Verification Checklist

  Run this before publishing a GitHub Release. Prefer a **clean Windows 11 x64 VM** (or a fresh
  user profile) so runtime detection and the PATH broadcast are genuinely exercised.

  ## A. Build artifacts (build machine)

  - [ ] `pwsh -File build/publish.ps1` succeeds; `publish/gitdelta.exe` exists and is ~5–15 MB.
  - [ ] `publish/` contains no per-app managed `*.dll` siblings (single-file bundling confirmed).
  - [ ] `& publish/gitdelta.exe --version` prints the expected version and exits without a window.
  - [ ] `pwsh -File build/make-installer.ps1` produces `installer/Output/GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe`.

  ## B. Clean-machine install (test VM WITHOUT .NET 10 runtime and WITHOUT gitdelta on PATH)

  - [ ] Copy `GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe` to the clean VM and run it (standard, non-admin user).
  - [ ] SmartScreen shows "Unknown publisher"; **More info → Run anyway** proceeds (matches README).
  - [ ] Installer runs **without a UAC elevation prompt** (per-user install).
  - [ ] If the bundled runtime is present: installer shows "Installing the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime..."
        and completes; if not bundled: the .NET download page opens at the end.
  - [ ] App installs to `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta` and `gitdelta.exe` is present there.
  - [ ] A **Start Menu** "GitDelta" shortcut exists and launches the app to the start screen.
  - [ ] **Settings → Apps → Installed apps** lists "GitDelta" with the correct version/publisher.

  ## C. PATH integration (test VM)

  - [ ] Open a **brand-new** PowerShell window after install (do not reuse a pre-install terminal).
  - [ ] `gitdelta --version` prints the version (resolves via PATH).
  - [ ] `gitdelta --help` prints usage to the terminal.
  - [ ] `gitdelta --version > out.txt` writes the version to the file (redirection works).
  - [ ] In a folder that IS a git repo, run `gitdelta` → app opens to **working-tree-vs-HEAD**.
  - [ ] In a folder that is NOT a git repo, run `gitdelta` → app opens to the **start screen**.
  - [ ] `gitdelta <path-to-repo>` opens that repo's working-tree view.
  - [ ] Inspect the PATH entry is a single, non-duplicated value:
        `(Get-ItemProperty 'HKCU:\Environment' Path).Path` contains `...\Programs\GitDelta` exactly once.

  ## D. Idempotent re-install (test VM)

  - [ ] Run the installer a second time over the existing install; it completes cleanly.
  - [ ] PATH still contains `...\Programs\GitDelta` **exactly once** (no duplicate appended).

  ## E. Uninstall (test VM)

  - [ ] Uninstall via Settings → Apps (or the Start Menu "Uninstall GitDelta" shortcut).
  - [ ] `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta` is removed.
  - [ ] Open a new terminal: `gitdelta` is no longer found (PATH entry removed).
        Confirm: `(Get-ItemProperty 'HKCU:\Environment' Path).Path` no longer contains the GitDelta dir.

  ## F. Git-missing path (optional, test VM without Git for Windows)

  - [ ] Launch GitDelta with git absent → the actionable "Git not installed" screen appears with a
        link to Git for Windows (per the spec's startup git detection).

  Only publish the release once every box in A–E passes.
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2: Execute the checklist once (MANUAL) and record results.**
  Spin up (or reset) a clean Windows 11 x64 VM. Build the installer on your dev machine with `pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1`, copy `installer/Output/GitDelta-1.0.0-setup.exe` to the VM, and walk through sections **A–E** of `docs/release-verification.md`, ticking each box. **Expected:** every box in A–E passes. Pay special attention to:
  - **C — new terminal:** the most common failure is testing PATH in a terminal opened *before* install; always open a fresh one.
  - **D — idempotency:** re-running the installer must not add a second `...\Programs\GitDelta` to PATH (this validates the `PathContainsDir` guard in `GitDelta.iss`).
  - **E — uninstall:** the PATH entry must be gone afterward (validates `RemoveDirFromPath`).

  If any box fails, fix the relevant script/`GitDelta.iss` from Task 11.1/11.2, rebuild, and re-run the affected section before committing.

  ```powershell

  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'

  Covers single-file publish, per-user install without admin, SmartScreen flow,
  .NET 10 runtime detection, PATH add (new-terminal) / idempotent re-install / removal
  on uninstall, and the gitdelta CLI fast-paths.

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

```
